President Chiang Personally Drafts Rules of Conduct

(Nanchang) President Chiang recently personally drafted rules of conduct to instruct the officers and soldiers of each army division and brigade to abide by them. They are recorded as follows: (1) Look at the big picture and start with the small details. (2) Do not be irresponsible. (3) Knowing is difficult, doing is easy. (4) Say you will do it, do it, and then talk about it. (5) Rewards and punishments should be clear, and kindness and authority should be combined. (6) Authority should be unified, and responsibility should be specialized. (7) Obey discipline and follow orders. (8) Do things in a step-by-step and orderly manner. (9) Do not do things perfunctorily. (10) Only fulfill my duties and responsibilities, do not shirk responsibility, and do not compete for credit. (11) Look for things to do, do not wait for things to do. (12) Talk less and do more. (13) Do not be ambitious and unrealistic, or change your mind easily. (14) Being loyal to your duties is being loyal to the revolution. (15) Do things smartly and concisely. (16) Sacrifice everything and fight to the end. (17th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Xiao Kong's Bandits and Other Bandits Encircled and Suppressed

(Nanchang) According to a message from the Western Route Headquarters, when the Kong Xiao Gao Li gangs fled to Wuning, they were surrounded and attacked by the Second and Third Columns. The main force of the bandits suffered heavy losses and are still being pursued and suppressed. (17th Dispatch)

(Nanchang) The public training groups of the districts under the jurisdiction of each garrison area have successively reported their establishment, training the local militia to guard the highway bunkers. (17th Dispatch)

(Hankou) The bandits on the border of Hubei and Jiangxi have been suppressed by the Hunan army and fled back to the Yangxin area in southern Hubei and are being blocked and suppressed. (17th Dispatch)

He's Bandit Remnants Flee Back to Their Old Nest in Sangzhi

(Hankou) Wang Lingji telegraphed Hankou on the 17th, saying that Zhang Guoshou personally led more than 10,000 elite bandits in a frontal counterattack against our army. After several days of bloody fighting, our front line was consolidated, and the bandits were finally defeated. In this battle, our army suffered more than 1,000 casualties, and the bandits suffered countless casualties. In addition, He's bandit remnants fled back to their old nest in Sangzhi, and western Hubei is peaceful. (17th Dispatch)

Victory Report from Jiangxi Province on Bandit Suppression

Bandit Leader Li Sengui Captured and Executed on the Spot

(Nanchang) The headquarters, in recognition of the Zixi team's capture of Li Sengui, the chairman and workers' minister of the pseudo-Soviet government, specifically telegraphed an order to execute the bandit on the spot and to give the team 500 yuan in national currency as a reward. (17th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Nanchang) The military campaign to suppress bandits on the front lines has repeatedly achieved victories. The conversion institute of the headquarters has also received a large number of surrendered prisoners from the front lines. According to a surrendered pseudo-regimental political commissar, the current bandits have been severely suppressed by the National Army and are fleeing in a state of utter chaos. The internal situation is extremely empty, and the bandits' morale is dissipated, and they all wish to surrender to the National Army. (17th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Red Bandits Invading Kaihua Flee to Zihukou

(Hangzhou) More than 10,000 red bandits invaded the key passes of Daqiaotou and Wangban in Kaihua on the Zhejiang border from eastern Jiangxi. They were met by the Zhejiang Security Team, and 700 to 800 bandits were killed. Yu Jishi received a telegram from Jiang Zhiyong in Huabu today, stating that the bandits disturbing Daqiaotou fled to Zihukou and the Maling area on the morning of the 16th. Jiang is now stationed in Yancun to supervise the suppression and will soon be able to quell the disturbance. (17th Dispatch)

Yin Rugeng Temporarily Postpones Trip

Some Details Still Need to Be Negotiated with the Japanese

Memorandum to Be Signed Before the Takeover

(Beiping) Yin Rugeng had originally planned to go to Gubeikou today to handle the handover matters. However, because some details still need to be negotiated with the Japanese, he temporarily postponed the trip. Yin met with Japanese military attache Chai Shan this afternoon to discuss everything, and there has been considerable progress. It is reported that before the takeover of Gubeikou is implemented, representatives from both China and Japan will sign a certain memorandum for compliance. Relevant parties said that the takeover of Gubeikou can definitely be achieved before the 25th of this month. Currently, there are only some details that need to be carefully considered. Our side is ready for the takeover. Yin will go with the takeover personnel after finishing his affairs in Beiping to jointly handle the handover matters with the Japanese representatives. (17th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Tao Shangming came to Beiping a few days ago to report to the authorities on the progress of the takeover after the handover of Shanhaiguan was completed. Now that the matter is over, he will go to Tianjin within a few days to meet with Yu Xuezhong and then transfer to the Tangshan, where the commissioner's office is located. (17th Dispatch)

Liu's Bandits North of the Yellow River Have Been Cleared

Bandit Suppression Troops Ordered to Return to Defense

(Beiping) According to a telegram from Qinyang, Liu's bandits north of the Yellow River have been cleared. Each of the bandit suppression units are under orders from the Military Council to return to defense. He Zhuguo has ordered the railway bureau to allocate cars for use to return to the north for demobilization. In the past, in Daming, Puyang and other counties, three to four hundred other bandits have been discovered and He's army will supress them on their return journey. The communists in Dingzhou are stirred and have moved troops to supress them. Liu Guitang, Cui Bangjie, Liu Zihuan and other scattered remnant troops numbering around 300 men had crossed the Yellow River to the south bank, and all of their horses and mules were stuck in the mud on both banks and were unable to cross. He's army recovered nineteen of them near Jiaodui Kou on the sixteenth. (17th Dispatch)

Weng Wenhao's Condition Still Critical

Under Treatment at Kwong Chi Hospital in Hangzhou

(Hangzhou) After Weng Wenhao was transferred to Kwong Chi Hospital in Hangzhou, his fever was slightly higher in the morning. Fragments of his skull had pierced his brain. Niu Huilin examined him at 10:00 AM, but because Weng's body was too weak and he had lost too much blood, he refused to perform surgery. He administered a small amount of saline and glucose intravenously. Weng's daughter and son-in-law arrived in Hangzhou in the afternoon. At 4:00 PM, he spoke a few words. His condition was better in the evening, but he was still unconscious and had not emerged from danger. At 7:00 PM in the evening, Zhang Shouyong arranged for a German doctor to come to Hangzhou for consultation. (Seventeenth-day special dispatch)

(Hangzhou) Weng Wenhao, Director of the Geological Survey of the Academia Sinica and a famous international scholar, yesterday (the 16th) traveled from Nanjing to Hangzhou with a colleague surnamed Wang in a hired small chartered car along the Nanjing-Hangzhou National Highway. At noon, after passing Biao Xing, Wang disembarked to investigate the Changxing coal mine disaster, leaving Weng to travel alone to Hangzhou. At 3:00 PM, while passing Qianjin in Wuxing, the driver inadvertently crashed the car's front into the iron railing of Yang Bridge before reaching Daixi Station. The engine exploded, and the car overturned, causing Weng and another driver to strike their heads directly forward, resulting in severe injuries and unconsciousness. Around 4:00 PM, the last train from Hangzhou to Kaihu passed by and discovered the accident. Weng and the others were helped onto the train to be transported to Hangzhou for treatment. However, the train reached Sanqiaobu, and Weng had fainted several times, his life in danger. He was taken to the nearby Wukang County Hospital for treatment. Weng still could not regain consciousness. Fortunately, the driver's injuries were minor, and he was able to speak, stating that Weng was the Secretary-General of the National Defense Design Council. The county magistrate, Yu Jinglun, personally came to Hangzhou to invite a doctor from Kwong Chi Hospital. Chen Bulei, the Provincial Director of Education, was a fellow villager of Weng from Cixi. Upon receiving the news, he not only requested a famous doctor to rush by car to provide emergency treatment overnight but also telegraphed Dr. Niu Huilin in Shanghai to come to Hangzhou for treatment. The doctors arrived after 12:00 AM that night. Upon examination, Weng's pulse was 108, and his body temperature was 35 degrees Celsius. He had a laceration above his left eyebrow, injuries to his forehead, nose, and a split lip. Although his injuries were severe, they were not life-threatening. After a little over an hour, Weng and the driver were transported from Wukang to Hangzhou by car, arriving at Kwong Chi Hospital at 3:00 AM. This morning (the 17th), Chen Bulei and provincial government officials and acquaintances of Weng visited him one after another. (Seventeenth-day special dispatch)

(Nanjing) Minister of Education Qian Changzhao, due to Weng Wenhao's car accident and injuries, accompanied Shen Kefei, Director of Surgery at the Central Hospital, and Yang Gongzhao, Director of Investigation, and others to Hangzhou via the Nanjing-Hangzhou National Highway to express their condolences on the morning of the 17th. (Seventeenth-day special dispatch)

(Nanjing) The news of Weng Wenhao's car accident and injuries has shocked the academic and political circles in Nanjing, all of whom are concerned for his safety. It is reported that Weng has been sent to Kwong Chi Hospital in Hangzhou, and Niu Huilin from Shanghai has been telegraphed to go to Hangzhou for treatment. It is said that Weng's condition has not changed and is not life-threatening. (Seventeenth-day Central News Agency dispatch)

(Nanjing) President Wang telegraphed Hangzhou on the 17th to express his condolences for Weng Wenhao's accident while traveling by car. (Seventeenth-day Central News Agency dispatch)

Provincial System Reform Plan Seeks Opinions from Various Provinces

(Nanjing) The Provincial System Reform Plan was previously resolved by the Central Political Council. (1) The original plan will be distributed to various provinces by the Executive Yuan, with a deadline of three months for submitting opinions. (2) A letter will be sent to the Administrative Law and Regulations Consolidation Committee to submit the consolidated parts of the provincial and county systems to the meeting. (3) After the opinions of the provinces and the reports of the Administrative Law and Regulations Consolidation Committee are received, a committee will be appointed to draft the principles for revising the Provincial Organization Law. Current Commentary

The Prospect of the Anglo-Japanese Commercial Conference

According to foreign news, the Anglo-Japanese Commercial Conference held a preliminary meeting on the 14th of this month at the British Government's Department of Commerce in London. In addition to representatives from the industrial and commercial sectors of both countries, government-designated representatives attended the meeting as observers. It is reported that the main purpose of the meeting is to seek a satisfactory solution to the issue of commercial competition between the two countries. In other words, it is to discuss how to peacefully divide the world market. Japan is the most developed industrial country in the Far East, and Britain's influence in the Far East is also deeply rooted. The outcome of this conference will have a significant impact on the development of the Far Eastern market. It is safe to say that at a time when the economic war between Britain and Japan is intensifying, the sudden negotiation of an overseas market compromise movement is of great significance.

The close relationship between Britain and Japan has a long history. Before the First World War, due to the open and secret struggles between Britain and Tsarist Russia on the world stage, the Anglo-Japanese Alliance emerged. After the end of the Great War, as Japan's power gradually increased, Britain, in order to avoid the deterioration of its relations with the United States in the Far East, abolished the alliance. The Washington Naval Treaty set the ratio of capital ships for the British, American, and Japanese navies at 5, 5, and 3, and the relationship between Britain and Japan was no longer as harmonious as before. Over the past decade, the Japanese have been conserving their energy and vigorously developing their military. Recently, they have occupied Manchuria, coveted North China, and advocated the Monroe Doctrine of Asia, claiming to be the masters of the Far East. This has shaken the foundation of British power in the Far East. Not only that, but Japan has also taken advantage of the current development of its national strength to dump its cheap goods in various countries, almost everywhere conflicting with British goods and capital. Even in important British colonial markets such as India, it has engaged in ruthless competition, causing significant blows to British commerce. As a result, the relationship between Britain and Japan has become increasingly tense. For the past two or three years, the British have certainly wanted to thoroughly coordinate with Japan. However, the economic interests of Britain and Japan are intertwined, and even with the success of the Siram Conference in regulating the British and Japanese markets in India, there is still a need for London negotiations to promote cooperation in the world market.

Britain is a country with vast colonies, but internal unity is becoming increasingly fragmented. The rule of the London government is gradually feeling unsustainable. Therefore, the entire diplomatic policy of the British Empire, in addition to maintaining overseas sales and investment markets, must also take into account the situation of various colonies. Based on this principle, not only in India does it seek to maintain mutually beneficial coordination with Japan by compromising, but also for its entire overseas market, it is willing to open up within the possible scope to allow the Japanese to share a portion. However, the Japanese are not willing to accept such British generosity, believing that the coordination between the two countries should be limited to the British Empire, implying that the markets outside Britain, such as South America, China, and small European countries, still have the energy to compete for dominance. Therefore, although the London talks are currently underway, there are many hidden reefs ahead. We, as observers in a third-party position, believe that the establishment of a compromise between Britain and Japan to divide the market is unlikely. The cunning and calculating British still have the remaining strength to struggle.

The Entire US Navy Will Still Be Concentrated in the Pacific

Will Return After Atlantic Exercises

Twelve New Ships Join the Fleet

(Washington) According to an announcement today by US Fleet Commander Admiral Sellers, the entire US fleet, including the twelve newly added ships, will sail back to the Pacific after conducting exercises in the Atlantic this summer. Recent reports suggested that the reconnaissance fleet would remain stationed in the Atlantic after this summer's exercises, but this statement is no longer valid. The reconnaissance fleet has traditionally been stationed in the Atlantic, while the battle fleet has been stationed in the Pacific. Until two years ago, due to the instability in the Far East, the reconnaissance fleet was transferred to the West Coast. Admiral Sellers stated today that he has received orders that the newly added ships must accompany the entire fleet to the Pacific, including three new battleships, five new heavy cruisers, one new aircraft carrier, two new destroyers, and two new submarines. (Sixteenth-day National Telegram)

Britain Does Not Recognize the Puppet State

League of Nations Publishes British Government Documents

Postal Issue Submitted to Committee

(Geneva) The British government's unwillingness to take any action that implies recognition of the existing political situation in Manchuria is evident in a letter dated January 8th. The British government's letter included a letter from Fujiwara, Director of Postal Affairs in Changchun, dated September 16, 1933, requesting that Britain provide statistics in accordance with the provisions of the Universal Postal Union to settle transit fees for mail passing through (Manchukuo). The British government has requested the League of Nations to submit this matter to the Advisory Committee established on February 24, 1933, in order to clearly define the scope of the de facto relationship allowed between foreign post offices and Manchukuo post offices without involving recognition of the current system in Manchuria. League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol has now convened the Advisory Committee to consider this matter on May 14th. This Advisory Committee was established to advise the League of Nations Assembly and to assist the Assembly in supervising the implementation of resolutions passed by the League of Nations Assembly regarding the Sino-Japanese dispute. (Seventeenth-day Reuters dispatch)

(Geneva) The League of Nations today focused on the dispute between the British and (Manchukuo) post offices. The (Manchukuo) post office transmits British mail, and the British post office also transmits mail from (Manchukuo). This has been the practice for some time. However, (Manchukuo) recently requested the British post office to fill out certain necessary statistics under the Postal Union, so the British government has requested the League of Nations to determine the extent to which relations can be established with the (Manchukuo) post office without involving recognition of (Manchukuo). It seems that (Manchukuo) wants to use this as a test case to gain recognition at least in postal matters. (Seventeenth-day Reuters dispatch)

Anglo-French Disarmament Talks

Doumergue Hosts Eden

(Paris) Prime Minister Doumergue is scheduled to host British Lord Privy Seal Eden at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs this afternoon. Anglo-French talks on disarmament are scheduled to begin after the banquet this afternoon. This morning at 11:45 AM, Doumergue and ministers without portfolio Herriot and Théodore, as well as the ministers of the various defense departments, held a meeting in the Prime Minister's office. Prior to this, Doumergue had also held lengthy consultations with Foreign Minister Barthou, Secretary-General of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Léger, and the French representative to the Disarmament Conference, Massigli. (Seventeenth-day Havas dispatch)

(London) British Foreign Secretary Simon gave a speech in Brighton today, mentioning the issue of disarmament and raising a question: What is the point of making proposals that great powers should disarm to the level of Germany, knowing full well that the great powers cannot accept them? Can the United States or Japan agree to it? If countries can reach an agreement to limit armaments, it will mark a new era in world history. If efforts in this regard fail, the world will once again fall into an unrestrained competition in the manufacture and deployment of war equipment, the consequences of which are beyond our prediction. (Sixteenth-day Reuters dispatch)

(London) Under-Secretary of State for Air Sassoon gave a speech at the Oxford Conservative Association today, advocating for the development of the British Air Force in clear terms. He stated that Britain only has 200 military aircraft for frontline combat, while the closest neighboring country has 997. Given the current situation in Europe, this situation is absolutely unacceptable. Britain's unilateral disarmament has reached its limit, and beyond this limit, it will be detrimental to national security. International peace cannot be guaranteed for the long term. If Britain mistakenly believes that the current state of peace is sustainable for the long term, danger will arise. In this situation, Britain should demand equality in air forces among all countries, and the way to achieve equality is to reduce the air forces of other countries to the same level as the British Air Force. As for military aviation, if it is abolished, the airspace over the territory will be controlled by countries with strong civil aviation, which is unacceptable to Britain. (Sixteenth-day Havas dispatch)

US Congressmen Propose Treasury to Buy Silver

London Silver Market Remains Firm

(Washington) Congressman Scrugham has introduced a bill in the House of Representatives proposing that the Treasury Department purchase at least 25 million ounces of silver per month for six months, and then continue to purchase 10 million ounces per month until the total amount of silver purchased reaches 1 billion ounces, or the gold-silver ratio reaches 16 to 1. The bill stipulates that if prices exceed the prices on January 1, 1926, the monthly purchase of silver can be reduced to 4 million ounces. The bill also stipulates that silver purchases should be paid for with silver certificates, which can be redeemed for silver bars at the then-current equivalent value of gold, and the redeemed silver certificates should still be used to purchase silver. Silver-backing congressmen in the House of Representatives have decided to establish a 100-member committee, led by Fessenden, and silver-backing congressmen have issued a resolution supporting the proposal to have the Treasury Department purchase 50 million ounces per month, up to 1 billion ounces, and this proposal stipulates that silver should be purchased at market prices and paid for with silver certificates, which can be redeemed for gold in the future. (Sixteenth-day Reuters dispatch)

(London) The London silver market has been firm recently because the public believes that the US government is being swayed by silver-backing congressmen and will soon take action. The future situation is still uncertain, but it is expected that the US government will purchase large quantities of silver stored in New York at a slightly higher price than the relatively open market. The recent weakness of the US dollar is likely due to American speculators buying British pounds in order to buy forward silver. However, London's purchase of gold is also a reason for the weakness of the US dollar, as the price of gold calculated in British pounds is almost the same as that calculated in French francs, so it is no longer profitable to buy French francs or withdraw cash from the Bank of France. The French franc expresses sympathy for the US dollar and continues to decline. (Seventeenth-day Reuters dispatch)

Near the state-owned tea plantations in Tiflis, Georgia, three large tea factories are currently under construction, with a total capacity of 6 million kilograms of tea leaves. The factories are equipped with various technologies, and the entire production process is mechanized. The production volume will be 3 million kilograms. (Sixteenth-day TASS dispatch)

Saitō Will Sacrifice the Education Minister to Preserve Everything

Although the issue does not have criminal implications in law, the fact that Hatoyama, the Education Minister, accepted bribes from a person involved in breach of trust and embezzlement, and was forced to attend the Investigative Committee under national scrutiny, is related to the dignity of the government, and its impact on the Saitō Cabinet is not insignificant. The government authorities seem to have made a major decision regarding the resignation of Education Minister Hatoyama to resolve all issues before the cabinet is affected. However, the outcome of the Investigative Committee will strengthen the momentum of all parties impeaching the current cabinet for its responsibility regarding discipline. New Commercial Treaty Signed: England and Russia Shake Hands Joyfully

Promotes Trade Balance Between the Two Countries

(London) No speeches were given at the signing of the Anglo-Russian commercial treaty. After the signing, British cabinet members shook hands joyfully with the Russian signatories. Regarding measures to balance exports and imports in 1938, one noteworthy point is that in 1933, Britain purchased a total of £17.5 million worth of Russian goods, while Russia purchased only £4.25 million worth of British goods. The treaty does not include any debt provisions, so it is generally regarded as temporary in nature. (Reuters, 16th)

(Moscow) Izvestia commented on the Anglo-Soviet commercial treaty, stating, "This agreement is the result of long-term negotiations and will undoubtedly satisfy those who wish to see the normal development and consolidation of Soviet-British economic relations. This commercial treaty contains real allowances for a substantial expansion of Soviet-British economic relations. However, we must understand that these allowances can only produce practical results under favorable conditions in the general relations between the two countries, and with the goodwill of both sides to act as a solid and correct foundation for these relations." The newspaper pointed out that Soviet-British trade had suffered serious setbacks in the past, but there is absolutely no conflict between the interests of the British national economy and the interests of the Soviet national economy. In the past, there have been many obstacles and misunderstandings in the path of normal development of Soviet-British commercial relations. The signing of this treaty will eliminate them. The newspaper concluded, "Soviet public opinion will certainly be satisfied with the signing of this treaty, because we all hope that this treaty will not only restore the foundation for the solid and normal development of Soviet-British commercial relations, but also serve as a pivot for the transformation of the entire Soviet-British relationship. This improvement is entirely in line with the wishes expressed by the Soviet government." (TASS, 17th)

Socialist Leader Flees to Czechoslovakia: The Great Powers Clear Up Matters Regarding Austria

Italy Intends to Issue Declaration to Aid Austrian Independence

England and France Have Different Views on the Method

Vienna Although the defeated Socialist Party is still resisting the government with guerrilla tactics, it is nothing more than embers after a great fire. More than 2,000 party members are now being detained for trial.

According to a Reuters correspondent in Paris, the French capital is now very concerned about the possible developments in Austria. Diplomats from France, England, Italy, and Czechoslovakia actively consulted on this issue yesterday. It is reported that the governments of France, England, and Italy intend to issue a joint declaration stating their determination to maintain Austria's independence. The Foreign Affairs Committee of the French Senate resolved to urge the government to assume the obligations of the Treaty of Versailles to protect Austria's independence, and to request a joint response to the appeal of Austrian Chancellor Dr. Dollfuss to convene a League of Nations meeting as soon as possible.

At the same time, a Reuters correspondent in Rome also telegraphed that the Italian government may request the League of Nations to investigate whether Czechoslovakia was involved in the Austrian turmoil, but this application will only be made after Chancellor Dollfuss implements his determination to resolve the Austrian issue through the League of Nations.

The Italian government has proposed that the three countries, England, France, and Italy, simultaneously issue communiqués in their respective capitals, announcing that the three countries share the desire to respect Austria's independence and territorial integrity. Italy made this suggestion to prevent rumors from arising that the three countries have differing opinions on the fundamental principles of this matter. It is noted that Chancellor Dollfuss previously announced that Austria intended to appeal to the League of Nations, and after England, France, and Italy replied, it was discovered that their opinions were not consistent. Italy does not particularly approve of this appeal. Parisian sources believe that even if the three countries issue a declaration respecting Austria's independence and territorial integrity, Austria may still seek assistance from the League of Nations at any time. (Reuters, 16th)

(London) The Italian government drafted a declaration stating that if Austria is subject to foreign interference, England, France, and Italy would guarantee its independence and territorial integrity. It asked England and France to join in order to issue it jointly. England and France have refused because this move implies supporting Dollfuss's policies. It is reported that the British government refused this request because Prime Minister MacDonald was angered by Dollfuss's domestic policies. If England is required to join, there must be a statement on this point. It is reported that France holds the same attitude. (National Telegram, 16th)

(Berlin) This dispatch received a Parisian telegram that French Foreign Minister Barthou's attempt to contact the British, Italian, and Czech governments to jointly issue a declaration to maintain Austria's independence has failed. The negotiations that Barthou conducted with the ambassadors and ministers of those countries in Paris broke down at midnight. Berlin newspapers stated that British Minister Eden arrived in Paris last night. It is claimed that Britain has no intention of supporting France's proposal because this move is of no practical help and will only provoke Germany. Italy had previously proposed that the powers maintain Austria's independence by force, but this was also blocked by the British ambassador because Britain does not want to be drawn into a whirlpool that could cause conflict on the European continent. (National Telegram, 17th)

Austrian Independence: An Element of European Equilibrium

French Parliament Resolves to Maintain the Treaty

England, France, Italy, and Czechoslovakia Have Also Guaranteed It

(Paris) Recent foreign reports say that negotiations are underway between London, Paris, and Rome, with the intention that the three countries simultaneously issue a declaration recognizing the need to respect Austria's independence and territorial integrity. The negotiations could reach a result soon. This news has been confirmed today and yesterday. The proposal to issue the declaration originated in Rome, and the attitudes of various countries are related to the recent events in Austria. Although the countries are paying close attention to Austria's fate, they inevitably hesitated slightly regarding the actions to be taken. However, since the recent uprisings of the Socialist Party in Vienna and Linz, the countries have no longer hesitated. The Austrian government had previously sent the governments of England, France, and Italy case files regarding the German National Socialist Party's disturbances in Austria, and at the same time declared that Austria intended to seek justice from the League of Nations. The three governments have replied to Austria's communication. The three governments, in principle, expressed sympathy for Austria, but their opinions on the methods to protect Austria's independence differed greatly. Italy continued to express doubts about seeking justice from the League of Nations. The wording of the three countries' replies was different, and there was concern that it would be exploited by others if it were published in the future. Therefore, the Roman government proposed that the three governments, in completely identical language, simultaneously issue declarations in the three capitals, expressing the three countries' shared desire to guarantee Austria's independence and territorial integrity. After this expression, the saying that maintaining Austria's independence is only a secondary matter for the countries can be disproved. This declaration will also not hinder Austria's seeking justice from the League of Nations. (Havas, 16th)

(Paris) The Foreign Affairs Committee of the Chamber of Deputies held an extraordinary meeting to study the Austrian events and unanimously passed a resolution requesting the government to guarantee Austria's independence in order to maintain peace. The Foreign Affairs Committee of the Senate also believes that Austria's independence and territorial integrity are necessary conditions for maintaining peace and preserving the European equilibrium. The peace treaty guarantees it, and the protocol signed by England, France, Italy, and Czechoslovakia in October 1932 also recognized that Austria should be protected, but its protection should be guided by the League of Nations and carried out within the scope of the League of Nations. No country may obtain special and unilateral benefits by protecting Austria. (Note: On July 15, 1932, England, France, Italy, and Czechoslovakia signed a protocol stipulating that Austria should receive international financial assistance. It was discussed by the Executive Yuan of the League of Nations on October 13 of that year.) Therefore, the Senate Foreign Affairs Committee unanimously believes that if Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss has appealed, then the countries that co-signed the protocol should promptly find ways to convene the Executive Yuan of the League of Nations in order to examine Austria's lawsuit and determine whether it is reasonable. The countries should also take the measures that the Executive Yuan may deem appropriate. (Havas, 16th)

Hitler States Germany Has No Connection to the Austrian Turmoil

Austrian Workers Will Inevitably Turn to National Socialism

(London) The Daily Mail's Berlin correspondent interviewed German Chancellor Hitler and published his remarks. According to Hitler, the recently signed German-Polish Non-Aggression Pact has absolutely no effect against the Soviet Union. He also said that the three Bulgarian Communist Party members who were arrested on suspicion of arson in the German Reichstag fire and subsequently acquitted by the Leipzig court will soon be released. When mentioning the Austrian events, he strongly denied that German National Socialist Party members were involved in the recent Austrian turmoil, and said that the German revolution had no riots or bloodshed, which was very different from the Austrian turmoil. Finally, he said that Austrian workers will inevitably turn to National Socialism in the future because the Austrian government has taken violent measures against the workers, which is bound to cause such a reaction. (Havas, 17th)

Austrian Government Reorganized: Fascist Faction Takes the Stage

Five Socialists Hanged

Cabinet Orders Partial Lifting of Martial Law

Denies Hundreds of Women and Children Died

Vienna At 8:20 last night, the Vienna Provisional Court again announced the death penalty for five people, who were sent to the gallows eleven minutes later. However, six other Socialist Party members, who were scheduled to be executed at midnight, were suddenly granted amnesty in the last few minutes.

This morning, the Cabinet issued an order that martial law be lifted in all provinces except Vienna, Upper Austria, Lower Austria, and Styria.

At 1:30 in the morning, the Cabinet decided to appoint Dr. Stummer as Minister of Social Welfare, while the incumbent Minister, Dr. Smidtz, was reassigned as Vienna Administrative Commissioner and Minister without Portfolio. This change is very significant because the new Minister of Social Welfare is recommended by the Austrian Fascist Heimwehr.

The Cabinet also decided to remove Socialist Party members from all parts of the country, so it ordered that all personnel invested or appointed by the Socialist Party be dismissed. This move will have a great impact because the newly appointed officials may dismiss civil servants affiliated with the Socialist Party.

The rumor in a certain foreign newspaper that hundreds of women and children were killed when the Vienna army bombarded is referred to here as false propaganda. It is said that a total of 137 civilians died in Vienna, of whom only nine were women and two were young children. The government is now trying to provide relief to the families of all innocent victims. (Reuters, 17th)

Vienna The Austrian Cabinet met from yesterday afternoon until 1:00 a.m. and then issued an order to lift martial law immediately in the provinces of Tyrol and Burgenland. Vienna, Upper Austria, Lower Austria, and Styria will also be lifted as soon as possible. The Cabinet also carried out a partial reorganization at the same time, appointing Stummer as Minister of Social Affairs, and the original Minister of the Department, Schmidtz, was reassigned to Minister without Portfolio. The Cabinet also ordered the cancellation of the qualifications of Socialist members of parliament and the dissolution of the Vienna Labor Bank. So far, seven people have been executed, and it is said that many more will be sentenced. The head of the Information Bureau, Lordwick, told foreign reporters that the rebellion has now been quelled. The recent turmoil has suddenly caused the Austrian royalists to show their faces. They declared that if Emperor Wilhelm of Germany had not been abolished in 1918, there would be no such incidents today. (National Telegram, 17th)

Vienna The government has recently ordered the dissolution of twelve Socialist Party organizations. Chancellor Dollfuss had previously issued a declaration to Socialist Party traitors, saying that traitors who handed over their weapons to the police would be granted amnesty. As of now, the traitors have handed over 73 machine guns, 3,276 rifles, 3,708 pistols, 204,000 rounds of rifle ammunition, 59,000 rounds of machine gun ammunition, and many hand grenades. (Havas, 16th)

Socialist Party Personnel Flee After Defeat: The Course of Escape

Underground Secret Passages in Vienna Lead to Sewers

Prominent Leaders Flee to Czechoslovakia One After Another

Vienna The Vienna Socialist Party apparently prepared a route for escape after failure when they launched their uprising, otherwise there would have been more deaths in this battle. Now, it has been found that the workers' residences destroyed by government artillery fire all have secret underground passages connecting to Vienna's underground sewers, which are as dense as a honeycomb. The defeated party members can walk through the sewers to a place farther from the battlefield and safely ascend to the ground through holes.

According to a Reuters correspondent in Prague, Austrian Socialist Party leaders Bauer and Dezh, after being forced to flee to Czechoslovakia, are now planning to move the headquarters of the Austrian Social Democratic Party to Brno. At the same time, a new Executive Committee has been organized in Vienna, and the matter is extremely confidential because if the committee members are detected by the authorities, they risk long-term imprisonment or even the death penalty. A total of 63 Austrian Socialists have fled to Czechoslovakia, and the authorities have confiscated their weapons and sent them to Brno. Mr. Dezh was injured in the fighting on February 13, the second day of the uprising, and is now staying in a sanatorium in Bratislava. Although he was injured, he walked all the way when he fled into Czechoslovakia, taking four hours to reach a safe place. (Reuters, 17th)

American Socialist Party Protests Against Austrian Government

Bloodshed Occurs During Gathering

(New York) Today, 20,000 Socialist Party members gathered in Madison Avenue Park for a meeting to oppose the Austrian oppression of the Socialist Party. A conflict suddenly arose, national flags were torn, and demonstrators picked up objects at hand to use as weapons. Chairs flew around, and there was a melee. Three women and nine men were beaten and injured, including two news photographers. One man was stabbed and seriously injured. It is now believed that about several hundred people suffered minor injuries. The situation reached its climax when 5,000 Communists tried to occupy the podium. There were only 170 police officers on duty at the scene, and they did not carry batons. The Mayor of New York and the Vice President of the Labor Federation had planned to attend the speech, but the riots had already broken out before they arrived. (Reuters, 16th)

Budapest, Hungary The Executive Committee of the Hungarian Social Democratic Party issued a declaration expressing solidarity with the Austrian Socialist Party. In addition, Congressman Pukingel, on behalf of the Socialist Party caucus in the House of Representatives, requested the Hungarian government to allow Austrian Socialist Party members the right to seek refuge in Hungary (Havas, 17th)

Newly Appointed Envoy to Portugal Zhang Xinhai Presents Credentials

Envoy Zhang has Very Harmonious Relations with Portuguese Diplomatic Circles

Will Use Lisbon Archives to Elucidate Chinese Culture

Lisbon Correspondence: Zhang Xinhai, Ph.D., the newly appointed Envoy Extraordinary and Minister Plenipotentiary of the National Government to Portugal, set sail from Shanghai last November and arrived in Lisbon in mid-December. On the afternoon of the twenty-seventh of that month, he presented his credentials to the Portuguese President. The Chief of Protocol of the Presidential Palace, Band Leit de Castro, led a cavalry escort to the Chinese Legation to accompany Envoy Zhang in the Presidential Palace's ceremonial carriage to the Palace. Envoy Zhang, accompanied by Secretary Wu Zhaohuan and Yang Xianzeng, entered to meet the Portuguese President, who paid his respects. Envoy Zhang then presented his credentials and read his credentials speech. After the Portuguese President read his response, he invited Envoy Zhang to sit for a while in his private office. After a long conversation, Envoy Zhang took his leave. Envoy Zhang then visited the diplomatic corps stationed in Portugal and met with all the envoys, especially the American envoy, who was very cordial. According to custom, a newly appointed envoy's initial meeting with other envoys is limited to a few words of greeting and does not involve lengthy conversations. This time, when Envoy Zhang first met the American envoy to Portugal, the American envoy specially arranged refreshments to entertain him, and his wife and daughter also sat with them, showing great cordiality, as if they were old friends. The American envoy also discussed with Dr. Zhang the richness of the Lisbon archives, which could be used for cultural reference between China and Portugal. Dr. Zhang is a scholar of Western literature. When he studied in the United States, his works were already well-known. The American envoy had long heard of his name, so upon meeting him, he engaged in a long conversation. Envoy Zhang has always been interested in anecdotes. Hearing the American envoy's words, he plans to use the Lisbon archives to further study the history of Sino-Portuguese relations during the late Ming Dynasty in order to elucidate Chinese culture, which has long been disseminated in the Atlantic countries. Portuguese Foreign Minister Medes and Undersecretary Santana, are both Portuguese scholars. Many members of the diplomatic corps in Portugal are also accomplished scholars. After meeting Envoy Zhang, they were in agreement and had very harmonious relations, which should have a considerable effect on future diplomatic relations.

Sun Dianying's Army Fully Attacks Ningxia

Yan Xishan Sends Troops to Assist in the Attack on Sun's Troops

The Elite of Sun's Troops is Almost Entirely Lost

Beiping Correspondence: The Ningxia war situation has not yet developed at present. The situation is recorded as follows:

Sun's Army Strategy: Sun Dianying has now returned to Shizuishan from Baofeng, still claiming to advance westward, leading his troops to besiege the provincial capital of Ningxia. However, fearing air raids, they move during the night and hide during the day. The Ningxia army's defenses are extremely strict, and Sun's army is not easily successful. Currently, Sun is at the end of his rope and lacks food, so he convened his subordinate generals in Shizuishan to discuss strategy. It was decided to launch a final fierce attack on Ningxia with all forces. If they occupy Ningxia, then Pingluo will fall without being attacked. However, food is lacking and this plan must be completed in the shortest possible time, otherwise the soldiers may desert. Therefore, a second step was decided: if the attack on the suburbs of Ningxia is not smooth, then they will lead the entire army around to Guyuan and Liangzhou to seek a way out. This is the reason for the Sun's army's two fierce attacks on the provincial capital of Ningxia in recent days.

Five Provinces Encirclement: Regarding the method of the five provinces encircling and suppressing Sun's army, although the Military Affairs Commission has ordered Jin, Sui, Gansu, Ningxia, and Qinghai provinces to prepare, it has not been implemented in practice. The crux of the matter lies in whether Shanxi will actually send troops to encircle and suppress. Now Yan has telegraphed the Ping Military Affairs Commission, saying that he has ordered the troops of Jin and Sui provinces to concentrate in the Wulin area on the twentieth of this month, and appointed Xu Yongchang and Fu Zuoyi as plenipotentiaries to go to Beiping for consultation. On the fourteenth, Fu Zuoyi telegraphed the Military Affairs Commission to report that he would go to Hebiancun to meet Yan and ask for instructions. The Military Affairs Commission believes that the movement of troops should be swift, and urgently telegraphed Xu and Fu to come to Beiping quickly to plan everything. They then received a reply that they would leave Bing by car together on the fifteenth at noon. It is heard that Yan has agreed to transfer three divisions and one independent brigade from Jin and Sui provinces to encircle and suppress Sun's troops, including Zhao Chengsui's cavalry division, Wang Jingguo and Fu Zuoyi's two infantry divisions, and Feng Yuxi's independent brigade, and has set a deadline of the twentieth of this month for them to concentrate in the Wulin area of ​​western Sui. Once Xu and Fu arrive in Beiping and agree on specific measures with the Military Affairs Commission, the troops from all directions will depart from western Sui. After Xu and Fu arrive in Beiping, they will discuss how to expedite the dispatch of troops and to what extent they will pursue and suppress Sun's army after the dispatch of troops. Therefore, Xu's mission to Beiping this time is very important.

The Beiping Military Affairs Commission will no longer issue a punitive order for the five provinces to encircle and suppress Sun's troops. The entire Guan Division stationed in the suburbs of Ping, as well as a cavalry regiment and an artillery regiment of the Liu Division, will also be ordered to go to Baotou. Currently, the Guan and Liu Divisions have issued a preparation mobilization order, and the soldiers' leather clothing has been made and the vehicles have also been prepared. A part will be sent first in the coming days.

Hankou Police Department Cracks Horse Racing Course Robbery Case

Four Robbers Arrested and Stolen Money Recovered

Hankou Correspondence: On January 2 this year, a robbery case of over ten thousand yuan occurred at the Hankou International Racecourse. It has now been cracked by the Garrison Department. The two masterminds and two perpetrators have been arrested. One person was murdered by accomplices and one is at large. The cracking of this case is bizarre and tortuous. I will record the main points as follows:

It turned out that the bandits Wang Xianzhang and Xue Yaoting were originally soldiers, formerly under the command of Fan Zhongxiu of the Jianguo Army. Wang was a regimental commander and Xue was a battalion commander. Fan died in the battle to suppress Feng Yuxiang, and the troops dispersed. Wang and others hid in Hankou, making a living by selling morphine. They often associated with bandits. One day, they gathered at Wang's residence at No. 81 Changqing Lane in the French Concession and decided to rob the International Racecourse. Wang and Xue masterminded the plan, while Ding Yuzhai, Tian Huating, Ren Qichang, and others were responsible for carrying it out. At that time, the people of Hankou were celebrating the New Year, and the entire city was in a frenzy. The garrison troops were maintaining security in the urban area, while the International Racecourse happened to be outside the urban area, so the bandits took advantage of the opportunity to jump into a car at 5 pm on the second, when the horse racing association personnel were carrying money out, and forced them to get out of the car with guns, ordering the driver to change direction. On the way, they smashed the box and robbed 13,103 yuan in cash. The Police Department, according to the reports of the Chief of the Investigation Division Ren Benzhao, the Commander of the First Regiment of the Garrison Brigade Shen Cheng, the Director of the Hankou Public Security Bureau Chen Xizeng, and the Manager of the Racecourse Chen Youxin, successively, ordered the Investigation Division to solve the case, and offered a reward of 500 yuan, in order to recover both the people and the stolen goods. After receiving the order, the Investigation Division divided into seven groups and mobilized all personnel, but there were no signs for a long time. Later, according to a tip from an informant, Hou, a Henan man named Yang Huai Zhi and a Tian man were in the racecourse every day, and Yang was a bad person and should be responsible for this. Therefore, Yang was arrested. According to the report of the manager of the Racecourse Chen Youxin, the four robbers all spoke with a northern accent. The driver Zhou Rongye also firmly stated that the person who forced him with a gun was Yang Huai Zhi. The evidence was conclusive, and Yang could not deny it. However, although Yang was not a good person, he did not participate in this case, so it was difficult to get a real confession about the details of the case. He only said that Ding, Ren, and Xue were related. According to the confession, the Police Department arrested Guo Wenqi, Xue Yaoting, and Wang Xianzhang one after another. Wang confessed that Ding Yuzhai, Tian Huating, and Ren Qichang were all in Anlu. He heard that Ren had been murdered by Ding, Tian, and others. The Police Department sent officers to Anlu with the criminal Wang to identify and arrest them. Because Ding and others were in the garden, they went to the garden to find Ding and Tian. Ren was indeed murdered. After Ding and Tian were escorted to Hankou, they were sent to the military court for interrogation together. Combining the confessions of the criminals, it was learned that the masterminds of this case were Wang and Xue. Wang and Ren looked for partners, Xue and Ren put together guns, Ding and Tian and a bandit from Nanyang and others robbed. Afterwards, they divided the spoils in Wang's residence, one share per person and one share per gun, totaling eleven shares, each share worth 600 yuan. The bandit who forced the driver was Ding Yuzhai. The driver Zhou Rongye, who insisted that Yang Huai Zhi was the one, actually mistook Ding for Yang, because the two had no difference in appearance or accent. Yang was innocent. But if Yang had not been arrested, the case would not have been solved. It was a strange event. When Guo Wenqi was arrested, 270 yuan of stolen cash was found, which was stored by Ding and was not a perpetrator of the robbery. Xue's stolen money, 340 yuan was deposited in the Zhongnan Bank and 1,200 yuan was deposited in the Zhejiang Industrial Bank, all of which were submitted in writing. Tian's stolen money was sent to his family for 400 yuan. There is also a wanted criminal who remitted 1,800 yuan of stolen money to Ping through the Jin Cheng Bank and took a car to the north. His two pistols were deposited in the Joint Office of the Military at Jincheng Lane and the secretary Zhang Yaonan's place. After the incident, Zhang also fled far away, and the guns have been searched and turned over to the police. The Police Department, with the case clear, will announce the verdict in the coming days. Wang, Xue, Ding, and Tian will all be severely punished in order to issue a clear warning. (February 17)

Songjiang

Preparing to Dredge Rivers and Measure Tributaries

The county government recently convened various sectors and decided to dredge the city moat. A river dredging committee has been organized at Quanjietang and is scheduled to start work on the 20th. Internal staff will be appointed by the director and reported for approval, and preparations will be made separately. The cost of dredging the river is estimated to be 70,000 yuan. Half of the funds will be raised according to the established precedent of collecting donations from annual rent payments, and the remaining funds will be borrowed from road construction funds and other funds. County Magistrate Jin sent Wei Jinsheng to meet with Director Shen of the Construction Department in person to request a payment order. It is now learned that he has been approved. After stating the reasons and submitting them to the department for instructions, the funds can be collected. In terms of engineering, the main river has been surveyed by the director of the county government's technical office, and the depth of dredging according to the original slope has been determined in sections, and a list has been drawn up for bidding for labor. The measurement of each tributary will also begin. Li Zufu, the district chief of the first district, will send personnel to accompany and provide instructions. The tributaries are Bailongtan River, Yangjiaqiao River, from Black Fish Lane to the west, to Bailongtan, then north from Hulong Bridge, to Tong'antangqian, west from Denlong Bridge to the west, along Dujiatan to Taqiao River, south from the Second Higher Primary School to the south, to Yangjiaqiao, then from Yangjiaqiao to Zerunqiao River, Songjiaqiao River, starting from behind Changqiao Street, south to Drunk White Pool, then to Jinshatan, Cangcheng River, starting from the Xiaocangqiao port, to Honglanganqiao. The surveying and mapping staff will lead three surveyors to start measuring each tributary immediately. The committee will divide the city into twelve towns, and each town chief will be responsible for raising funds to facilitate the project.

Wuxi

Survey Record of Profits and Losses in Various Industries

Wuxi is a prosperous commercial area, but since the floods in Jiangnan and the January 28th Shanghai Incident, the rural economy has been extremely devastated, the market has declined, and the various industries have been greatly affected. Now, after the end of the year, I will record the profits and losses of the various industries as follows: (1) Qian Industry: There are a total of fourteen companies in the city engaged in remittance and lending. Since the silk industry failed the year before last, most of them have been affected. Last year, they all engaged in contraction and were lifeless. The loans made were only one-third of what they were in the past. Only Fuyu, Fuchangsheng, Fuyuan, Yichang, Shenyu, and a few other companies were able to make a small profit. In addition to this, it was only enough to cover expenses. There are still several companies with a larger scope on weekdays, because they have been most affected, and whether they can operate as usual or liquidate their accounts will depend on the final outcome in the future. (2) Rice Industry: Wuxi is a rice-gathering area. There are more than 200 rice shops in the city, combined into eight sections. Recently, affected by the dumping of foreign rice and the consecutive years of good harvests in the country, the rice market has fallen to the extreme. The rice shop business is far from what it used to be. Most of the shops are losing money, with only Beitang Longmao, which specializes in soybeans, making a profit of 10,000 yuan. In addition, Dedayuan, Dinghe, Hefengtai, and Yuanhe in the Sanliqiao section, Yuanda and Changtai in the Huangniqiao section, Zhang Baotai and Changji in the Beizhakou section, and Hengshun in the Ximen section, and Baolong and Zhang Yuchang in Nantang all made a profit of several thousand yuan. The rest are difficult to profit. (3) Silk and Cloth: The industry has been continuously reducing prices since the spring, so the business is very prosperous. At the end of the year, Shihe, Rixin, and Shitaicheng are the best, each with a profit of 10-20,000 yuan. In addition, Jiuyu, Maolun, and Daxin all made a profit of several thousand yuan. (4) South goods: The business of this industry has always been the most lively at the end of the old calendar year. This year, the weather is sunny and the year is fruitful, so the business is also prosperous. Companies such as Wanda, Tianlai, Sanyang, and Yida have profits. (5) Flour: Since the September 18th Incident, the Northeast market has been completely seized by Japan. The flour industry has been most affected. In addition, the increase in donations and taxes has increased costs, making it impossible to sell. Inventories are piled up, and the economic impact is even greater. Therefore, they stopped the machines early to avoid being overwhelmed by flour. Regarding the situation of the factories, only Jiufeng had a slight profit. Maoxin's one or two factories usually sell flour in large quantities to the Northeast. Now, sales are sluggish, so it is only enough to cover expenses. Tailong must have lost tens of thousands of yuan.

The Bureau of Reconstruction Receives Orders to Resume Operations

Due to the importance of local construction projects, Shen Baixian, Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Reconstruction, has specially formulated regulations to change the current organizational principles for construction matters in various counties of Jiangsu Province. The regulations stipulate the abolition of all county technicians' offices. Counties with a total annual construction revenue of over 60,000 yuan, or those with particularly important construction projects, may establish a Bureau of Reconstruction. It is stipulated that six counties, including this county, Wuxian, Nantong, Rugao, Jiangdu, and Zhenjiang, establish Bureaus of Reconstruction. The position of Director of the Bureau of Reconstruction in this county has been entrusted by Director Shen to Zhang Fulin, the current Chief of Technical Affairs of the County Government. This appointment has been submitted and approved by the 634th Provincial Government Committee meeting. As for the date of establishment, the Department of Reconstruction originally stipulated early March, but due to the fact that all preparatory procedures may not be completed in time, the establishment must be postponed until mid-March.

Changzhou

An Overview of the General Year-End Closing for Various Industries

Before January 28th, most industries in Wu County, regardless of the type, generally had surpluses. However, after January 28th, most industries experienced losses rather than profits, and were further affected by the overall collapse of the money-lending industry. Consequently, most industries lost their ability to manage their finances, and business plummeted. Therefore, apart from the bean, lumber, and dyed cloth industries, there is virtually nothing else worth mentioning in terms of profits during this year-end closing. The bean industry's business in 1933 was unprecedented. This was due to an exceptionally good bean harvest in northern Anhui and this province, coupled with the fact that the supply of Dalian beans dwindled after the boycott of enemy goods. As a result, beans from northern Anhui and this province were in great demand for a time, with an average sales volume of over two million piculs. Cuichang was the leading company in this industry, followed by Jintai and Tongchang. The lumber industry has traditionally been a major business in Wu County. Business was still good last year, and the financial situation has improved, so there were profits. The dyed cloth industry benefited from extensive sales in northern Jiangsu, and the financial situation was also good, resulting in considerable profits.

In order to improve the production sector, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Reconstruction has specifically organized an Industrial Improvement Committee. Fugitives Transferred to the Court

Cai Deyuan, a native of Wu County, Anhui Province, was previously arrested at the train station for selling counterfeit money and transferred to the court. After the investigation was completed, he was sentenced to two years and six months in prison. After the sentence was confirmed, he was transferred to prison to serve his sentence. However, Cai took advantage of the guards' negligence some time ago, dug a hole, and escaped, also taking Xia Xiaobao, a fellow prisoner, with him. Subsequently, they were captured separately by county government police informants, brought back to the county for interrogation and detention. Zhenjiang Prison, considering that Cai and others had committed the crime of escaping from prison, specifically sent a letter to the court yesterday to handle the case according to the law. The prosecutor's office immediately opened a court to investigate the case and ordered their detention pending investigation and legal action.

Jiangyin

Economic Decline and Business Stagnation

Cheng County's businesses, adhering to customs, still carried out their year-end closing on the thirteenth day of the second month. However, due to the impact of the rural economic decline, all industries are stagnating. Only three financial institutions remain: Yongcheng, Xiecheng, and Taiji. During July and August, the orders for cloth mills were very enthusiastic. Huacheng alone had seven to eight million in sales for the entire year, but it was slightly affected during the Fujian Incident. The yarn mills' business was still good in the first half of the year, but inevitably less so in the second half. Due to the low selling price of rice, few rice merchants made profits. Since the launch of automobiles, the number of passengers on inland river boats has dropped sharply. The Cheng Yu and Cheng Wu lines are barely operating, and the Cheng Xi line has virtually stopped. The silk and cloth business is difficult to maintain. Wanyusen Yongsheng in the city and Jinyusen Qiafengxiang outside the north gate have all announced liquidation. Zhicheng Company, a printing business, has suffered heavy losses, and the shareholders' meeting has decided to liquidate, resulting in the indefinite suspension of the publication of newspapers that uphold justice.

The Ministry of Finance's Taxation Administration Revises Import Match Tax Rates

Orders Have Been Issued Separately to Comply

Since the Ministry of Finance revised the import tax rate on matches on November 5 and increased the consolidated tax, imported matches have taken the opportunity to dump their products, which has greatly affected the domestic match industry in Hebei, Shandong, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui provinces, almost to the point of being unable to maintain itself. The match industry associations of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui provinces have specifically organized an association to actively carry out a tax reform movement. Now the Taxation Administration of the Ministry of Finance has submitted the revised method of levying taxes on imported bulk matches and flat-box or booklet-style matches to the Ministry of Finance for circulation and implementation, so as to be fair and equitable. Yesterday, I found two documents from the Taxation Administration and copied them as follows:

Revised Tax Rate for Bulk Matches

The Taxation Administration of the Ministry of Finance orders all regional bureaus to revise the tax calculation standards for imported bulk matches. The original text states that the tax rate for bulk matches listed in Item E of Article 3 of Chapter 2 of the Consolidated Match Tax Collection Regulations previously issued by the Administration, which is 1.25 yuan per 100 catties (i.e., 60.48 kilograms), refers to the bulk matches that are poorly made three-headed and four-headed matches and incomplete matches produced by domestic manufacturers, and stipulates that they are limited to sales in the local area and are not allowed to be transported to other places for sales. Complete bulk matches cannot be handled in the same way. Now it is found that imported matches are sometimes imported in bulk, and they are complete and tidy matches. It is urgent to formulate another tax calculation standard in order to collect taxes and prevent abuses. Now it is found that the weight of the matches in each large box (i.e., 7,200 small boxes) of Grade B and C matches (excluding the leather box) is about 48 catties. For the sake of fairness, the Administration intends to use this weight as the standard. Hereafter, whenever imported bulk matches are imported, regardless of the length of each match, each unit will be uniformly calculated as 48 kilograms, and the national currency of 21 yuan should be levied according to the newly revised safety match Grade C tax rate. If there is an excess or a deficiency, it should still be levied proportionally in order to be fair and equitable. In addition to informing the Customs Administration to inform all customs offices and issuing separate orders, the bureau director and the director of the bureau are also instructed to inform and instruct all their subordinates to be informed. This order,

Flat Box and Booklet-Style Match Tax

At the same time, all regional bureaus were ordered to formulate the tax collection methods for imported flat-box and booklet-style matches. The original text states that the Administration's collection of consolidated match taxes has always been handled in accordance with the fixed rules. However, it is found that the box-packed matches of imported safety matches are quite inconsistent. Some are packed in flat boxes, and some are packed in booklet-style. The review is inconsistent with the fixed rules. In order to facilitate tax collection, it is urgent to formulate another collection method to show flexibility and to be uniform. Now it is proposed that for imported flat-box matches, if the volume of each small box is between 48 millimeters and 59 millimeters, and the width and thickness are two degrees, and the number of matches in the box does not exceed the Grade A regulations and is less than 100, each unit (i.e., 7,200 small boxes) should be levied 17.4 yuan of consolidated tax according to the currently stipulated safety match Grade B tax rate. For booklet-style matches, it is now proposed to calculate according to weight. Each 48 kilograms (including the leather), the national currency of 21 yuan should be levied according to the current safety match Grade C tax rate. If there are any odd lots, they should still be levied proportionally in order to be fair and equitable. If imported matches are subsequently encountered, and the width and thickness of the box are less than the Grade A regulations, they should still be taxed according to Grade A. If the volume of the box exceeds the Grade A regulations by one degree, even if it is less than Grade B, it should also be taxed according to Grade B, and so on. As for the number of matches in each box, if it exceeds the scope of each grade's regulations, the tax should be increased by one grade in accordance with the regulations to prevent cheating. In addition to submitting a report to the Ministry for record and informing the Customs Administration to inform all customs offices and issuing separate orders, the bureau director and the director of the bureau are also instructed to inform and instruct all their subordinates to be informed. This order,
