The Navy's Chongyi Gunboats Launched Yesterday

Wang Shouting Chaired, Students From Tongji Threw Bottles

The Self-Made Jiangfeng Aircraft Flew Around the Ceremony Site

Navy Chief Chen Shaokuan Came to Shanghai From Beijing to Participate

The Navy Department's Ning-class gunboats No. 7 and No. 8, Chongning and Yining, were laid down on November 12 last year, the anniversary of the death of the Prime Minister, and were built by the Jiangnan Shipyard. The launching ceremony was held at 3:30 PM yesterday. Wang Shouting, Commander of the Training Fleet of the Navy, chaired the ceremony.

Ceremony Site Arrangement

The site was located east of the No. 3 dock of the Navy's Jiangnan Shipyard in Gaochangmiao, in front of the Chongning and Yining gunboats. A temporary platform was built with wooden planks, about three zhang long, one zhang wide, and five chi high. In the center hung a portrait of the Prime Minister and the flag of the party and the country. National flags were hung around the platform. Ye Baoqi, the commander of the Navy Guard Battalion, led a team of soldiers to strictly guard the ceremony site. At the same time, all the soldiers of the Hai Rong warship were armed and stationed next to the two gunboats.

Attendees

The attendees of the launching ceremony included Wang Shouting, Commander of the Navy Training Fleet, Chen Zaofan, Deputy Director of Jiangnan Shipyard, Ye Zaifu, Director of the Shipbuilding Department, Yu Jianfu, Director of the Business Department, Liu Wu, Director of the Inspection and Construction Department, Liang Xunying, Director of the Materials Department, Qiu Zizhong and Chen Yongqin, captains of the ships Yixian, Tongji, Hairong, Yongjian, Yongji, Zhongshan, Haining, and Suning stationed in Shanghai, officers from the Training Fleet Command and the First Fleet Command, and more than 1,000 employees, workers, and guests from the shipyard. Navy Chief Chen Shaokuan arrived in Shanghai from Beijing yesterday morning to participate in the ceremony.

Jiangfeng Flying Around

Zeng Yijing, Director of the Navy Aircraft Manufacturing Office, specially dispatched the newly renovated Jiangfeng aircraft, which had completed the land-based wheel and plate work, to be piloted by Xu Chengqi, an aviation instructor of the Ning Navy ship, during the launching ceremony of the Chongyi gunboats. The aircraft took off from Shanghai Huazhong Airport at 3:00 PM, flew in the sky above Gaochangmiao, and performed technical feats. After the launching ceremony was completed at 4:00 PM, it returned to the Aircraft Office in Gaochangmiao after landing at Longhua Airport.

Bottle Throwing Ceremony

The Chongyi gunboats were hung with party flags on top, national flags in the middle, and national flags all around. A bottle of champagne wrapped in five-color silk was hung on the bow of each boat. At 3:30 PM, Wang Shouting, Commander of the Training Fleet, presided over the ceremony as required. Then Liu Ronglin and Que Yi, students from the Tongji warship, performed the bottle throwing ceremony. First, Liu Ronglin threw the champagne bottle from the bow of the Chongning gunboat towards the bow of the boat. The champagne splashed everywhere, and amid the military music and applause, the boat entered the Huangpu River. At 3:35 PM, Que Yi threw the champagne bottle from the bow of the Yining gunboat in the same way towards the bow of the boat, and the launching was completed.

Completed in May

After being launched yesterday, the Chongyi gunboats were moored on the Jiangnan Shipyard's riverside in Gaochangmiao and were still being renovated by the shipyard. They are scheduled to be completed and hoist their flags in May of this year and be incorporated into the Navy's Coastal Defense Office. As for the ninth and tenth gunboats, Changning and Zhining, the keel laying ceremony has been scheduled for the 20th of this month and construction has begun. The boats are 140 feet long, 20 feet wide, displace 350 tons, have a draft of 6 feet, and a speed of 12 knots per hour.

Kong Xiangrong Reports in Detail on the Inspection of the River Closure Project

Transportation is Difficult, There is a Risk of Suspension Due to Lack of Materials

The Nature of the River is Changeable, Artificial Materials Must be Available

Inspector Liu Bingzhong is Sent to be Stationed at the Site Permanently

Kong Xiangxi, Chairman of the National Government's Yellow River Flood Relief Committee, attached great importance to the Yellow River closure project and the construction of water defense embankments on both sides of the river. He previously sent Kong Xiangrong, a member of the committee and chief inspector, to the Fenglou construction site to conduct an on-site inspection of the closure situation. It is reported that due to the small rise in the ice jam at the breach, the pile placement in the closure construction was washed away and is now being remedied. The time is approaching the ice flood season, and the influx of ice blocks is particularly noteworthy. In order to prevent accidents, Chairman Kong has forwarded the Chief Inspector's report to the committee's work relief group for review, and has sent Inspector Liu Bingzhong to be stationed at the site permanently to conduct inspections at any time to prevent unforeseen circumstances. The original text of the Chief Inspector's report is disclosed below:

In order to comply with the re-submission of the detailed situation of the project, I pray for your review. I, Xiangrong, was dispatched to Henan, Shandong, and Hebei provinces to discuss the fundraising methods for the Yellow River breach closure project and to inspect the progress of the closure project at the Fenglou breach. The reports have been submitted separately. I was also instructed to report the details of the project separately. According to the original method of the work relief group, the isolated trees in the water where the willow raft project has been done on the entrance dam are used as the starting point of one end, and the village slope on the opposite bank is used as the starting point of another end. At the same time, willow branches are arranged at both ends, and stones are pressed down to gradually increase the height and progress in turn. Two rows of piles are signed in the water to defend the work. It is heard that it was originally planned to store 8,000 cubic meters of stone materials for demand, and it is estimated that 1,600 cubic meters have been transported. (According to Engineer Qi's report) Except for the use of , there are only about 600 cubic meters left. (According to Engineer Song's report) Iron rails are being paved to prepare for transportation, but because there are not enough trains to allocate and ships are also difficult, the waterway is experiencing freezing, and there are many string ditches on the land road, transportation is inconvenient. Can

Wait for the material to be stopped? That is a question. This should be noted first. It was also found that 34 wooden piles were signed. (According to Engineer Qi's report) The day before Rong arrived at the construction site, eight wooden piles in the deepest part of the big flow were washed away by the ice jam, which was at an important part of the project, causing the two ends of the project to be unable to connect, and there were many obstacles to the progress. Remedial measures are being taken. It is heard that the spring roll method will be used (rolling stone blocks with willow branches or rolling soil bags with hemp bags to sink), but

The water flow is turbulent, and it is also in a deep flow. Can it withstand the flow and implement the closure? That is a question. This should be noted second. Furthermore, the Yellow River has excessive floating sand and the water is fierce. It is not suitable for long piles. It is heard that when Zhou Fuzhi managed the river, he mobilized pile drivers to drive long piles, but the result was a failure. Is it effective to use signing piles now? That is a question. This should be noted third. It is also found that the Yellow River ice flood will arrive in an instant, and the ice blocks will fall and the water level will rise. Both have great harm to the closure project. Can the closure project be completed before the ice flood? That is a question. Even if the closure is completed, can it withstand the damage caused by the water and the water is still running? and still not completed

When the ice flood arrives, is there any considerable preparation to prevent the project from being washed away and failing? That is another big question. This should be noted fourth. It is also found that if this closure project can proceed smoothly, be completed on schedule, and no accidents occur during the ice flood, it should also be noted

When the peach flood and the ambush flood are at high water level, can it be defended? The project here is one of the most important defense lines of the embankment project in the Shitou Zhuang Shuikoumen area. If this place is not defended, then the newly built project will be dangerous everywhere. How should we defend it to achieve perfection? That is another question. This should be noted fifth. In addition, the first diversion canal dug by the project site is too close to the mouth of the canal and has been silted up. The water flow of the second diversion canal is sometimes over and sometimes silted up.

Unimpeded blockage is uncertain. Rong, the inspector, Liu Bingzhong, stayed in Bian to inspect, so Engineer Song made an appointment to go to the breach to observe the current water situation. When he saw that the third diversion canal originally designated by the project site was not in the current direction, Engineer Song made an appointment with the officer to go to the site designated between the second and third diversion canals to sign the central pile of the diversion canal and hand it over to Engineer Li for measurement and construction as the third diversion canal. On the night of January 18, the head of the diversion canal was washed away by the river flow and flowed into the old course, reducing the amount of water at the third breach. The original third diversion canal, which is currently in the current direction, has now been changed to the fourth diversion canal.

Is being excavated for flood discharge. However, in order to maintain the current diversion canal flow and increase the depth, without causing multiple collapses on both slopes, it seems that the willow dam on the opposite bank of the second and third diversion canals should be prevented from advancing too much, causing the diversion canal slope to collapse and the river flow to be scattered and blocked. This should be noted sixth. In short, the closure project is related to the water situation, artificial materials, and the three are simultaneously related. It has been presented yesterday. Because the Yellow River's water is changeable, if the water situation is suitable and artificial materials are available, it will be effective to rush to build day and night. Therefore, the person in charge of the matter pays attention to this three times. All the details of the inspection of the closure project in compliance with the instructions should be submitted for review.

The Telephone Bureau Took Over the Pudong Telephone Yesterday Evening

Converted to Common Battery System and Switched From Branch Bureaus

Telephone Charges are Lower Than Before, Number of Users Increases

According to the temporary contract, the Ministry of Communications' Shanghai Telephone Bureau took over the Pudong cross-border telephone from the Shanghai Telephone Company at 8:00 PM yesterday evening. The telephones are all equipped with a common battery system. Director Xu Xueyu and others went to the Pudong Branch Bureau last night to inspect. The details are as follows:

Installed Common Battery System

The Shanghai Telephone Company's Pudong cross-border telephone has a total of 78 sets. Since the establishment of the Pudong Branch Bureau of the Shanghai Telephone Bureau, it has begun to convert the cross-border telephone to a common battery system. The branch bureau has sent craftsmen to convert the new users' telephones to a common battery system. More than 50 sets have been installed so far, totaling about 130 sets with the cross-border telephone. It is temporarily stipulated that numbers 1 to 70 are new telephone numbers, and numbers 70 to 150 are the converted numbers for cross-border telephones.

Took Over Last Night

At 8:00 PM yesterday evening, the Telephone Bureau took over the Pudong cross-border telephone, cut off the telephone line that directly connected the former concession to Pudong, and transferred it to the Pudong Branch Bureau for switching. When users in the concession want to talk to users in Pudong, they should first dial (04), which is the (04) manual station in the central Jiangxi Road of the telephone company, and then the operator will connect to the Pudong Branch Bureau and transfer to the Pudong user's number. When users of the Nanshi Zhabei automatic machine want to talk to users in Pudong, they should first dial (36), the number of the Pudong Branch Bureau, and transfer to the Pudong user. Jiangwan, Zhenru, Wusong, Longhua, etc., are all transferred according to the manual telephone usage method.

Director's Inspection

Xu Xueyu, Director of the Telephone Bureau, Yu Bingjian, Engineer, and others went to the Pudong Branch Bureau at 7:00 PM yesterday afternoon to inspect. After the official takeover, the staff of the Pudong Branch Bureau were very busy. The bureau has also reported the takeover process to the Ministry of Communications. As for the Pudong cross-river line, it was originally 150 pairs from the Telephone Company's Sanmalu Bund. Now it has been purchased by the Telephone Bureau, and 50 pairs have been added in Gaochangmiao, totaling 200 pairs. Pudong users can install a total of 600 households.

Low Telephone Charges

After the Pudong cross-border telephone was taken over by the Telephone Bureau last night, the telephone charges payable by users in February will still be collected by the Telephone Company before February 17, and the Telephone Bureau will collect them from February 18. When the Telephone Company charged before, due to the cross-river line relationship, the quarterly charge for users' residences, businesses, and factories was from 60 to 90 taels. Now the Telephone Bureau's charges stipulate that the monthly charge for Pudong users' residences is 12 yuan, and the monthly charge for businesses and factories is 15 yuan, which is much lower than before. Therefore, it is expected that the number of Pudong users will inevitably increase.

Two-Railways Administration Organizes Railway-Owned Properties

Reconstructing Destroyed Property Maps from the January 28th Incident

Renewing Lease Agreements and Clearing Arrears

The railway-owned properties of the Two-Railways (Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways) are scattered and fragmented. In addition, during the January 28th Incident, nineteen volumes of records and maps related to the properties were destroyed, making it difficult to investigate and verify. Therefore, it was decided to start with a thorough investigation to get to the bottom of the matter and take the opportunity to improve the situation. In addition to checking deeds and re-compiling lease agreements, work such as surveying and mapping land is currently underway.

Creating Land Maps

For the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway properties, the maps and records were retrieved from the Hangzhou Engineering Office to first reconstruct the maps of the railway properties. Then, according to the old lease agreements, maps of lease affairs and general maps of branch stations were created. For the properties of the Shanghai-Nanjing Main Line and the Songhu Branch Line, most of the original maps and records were destroyed, so they can only be re-surveyed for mapping. The original survey team personnel will be assigned to this task, and some engineering interns will be recruited to assist. Starting from the Songhu Branch Line’s Paotaiwan, the leased land area will be measured, and the maps of lease affairs will be reconstructed. At the same time, the names of tenants will be investigated, the boundaries of railway properties will be marked, and lists will be compiled for future reference. The Songhu Line has already been surveyed and is being annotated with standard scale sizes and re-calculating the area. Half of the Shanghai-Nanjing Line has also been surveyed. In total, more than 160 maps of lease affairs and more than ten station boundary lease affairs maps have been created for the main and branch lines. In another half year, all work can be completed. When the land maps and records are drawn in the future, maps of the respective cities and counties will be created and sent to the respective cities and counties for record-keeping to confirm property rights.

Renewing Lease Agreements

Due to years of unrest and the January 28th Incident, many lease agreements for leased railway land have been left un-renewed, and some have expired long ago without being renewed. First, expired lease agreements were checked, and the lease agreements that expired at the end of the 20th year of the Republic were urgently checked and sent for renewal. At the same time, the renewal of lease agreements that expired at the end of the 21st year of the Republic was carried out. In total, 1,216 of these lease agreements were sent for renewal in one year, and the work is still continuing.

Clearing Rent Arrears

Some tenants of the Two-Railways properties have been in arrears with their rent for as long as ten years. By the end of the 21st year of the Republic, the total amount of rent arrears reached a huge sum of seventy to eighty thousand yuan, and the number of tenants was also very large. In order to thoroughly clear the arrears, the lists were checked and listed by station, by tenant, by year, and by amount. The methods for collection were devised in order of importance. For example, the China Transportation Company owed more than thirty-five thousand yuan. After negotiations, the freight depot built by the company at the Shangbei Station was valued and transferred to the Administration. The insufficient amount was deducted from the deposited security deposit. Another example is the Hangzhou Waterworks renting land to build a factory, and the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway renting land to lay sidings. Lease agreements were negotiated and signed to collect rent and settle outstanding cases. As for the leased land in the Gaozi Longtan area, where there were no agreements or maps, making it difficult to collect rent, personnel were sent to identify the leased land area, tenant names, and sign agreements with attached maps, and re-determine rents to collect rent according to the agreement to clarify the situation. The arable land rented out at the entire Gongchen Bridge station had inconsistent elevations and rent disputes, which had been pending for a long time. An average rent method was properly drafted, and leases were renewed and rented out separately, completing everything.

Preparatory Meeting to be Held in Shanghai Early Next Month

Locations Chosen Include Yandang Mountain and Tiger Hill

According to the Dagong News Agency, Military Committee Chairman Chiang Kai-shek believes that the transportation industry is extremely important for promoting local culture, developing transportation, promoting commerce, facilitating military operations, preventing bandits, and consolidating security. In order to actively develop transportation between provinces, he specially ordered Zeng Yangfu, the director of the border highway offices of the five southeastern provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Fujian, Anhui, and Jiangxi, to complete all the highways that have been rushed to build by June of this year, so that thousands of miles of highways between provinces can be fully connected and unimpeded. The Southeast Transportation Exhibition will be held in mid-June, along various highway lines. The locations will be Yandang Mountain and Tianmu Mountain in Zhejiang Province, Tiger Hill in Jiangsu Province, Longhu Mountain in Jiangxi Province, and Dashan Ridge in Fujian Province, etc. The exhibition period will be set for 20 days. Materials for the exhibition, such as local specialties, terrain, history, customs, etc., will begin to be collected. After receiving the order, Director Zeng Yangfu, considering the importance of the matter, plans to convene a preparatory meeting in Shanghai in early March at the office of the National Economic Council, inviting Chairman Chen Guofu of Jiangsu, Director Shen Baixian of the Construction Department, Chairman Liu Zhenhua of Anhui, Chairman Chen Yi of Fujian, Chairman Xiong Shihui of Jiangxi, Chairman Lu Dipin of Zhejiang, and the heads of highway bureaus from various provinces to attend. The ship is 190 feet long, 26 feet wide, with a total tonnage of 1097 tons, a speed of 11 miles, a novel style, unique design, spacious passenger seats, and extremely perfect content. The bureau sent invitations to all sectors to visit in advance, so more than 1,000 people arrived at the time, such as Director Xu of the Municipal Public Works Bureau, Deputy Director Gao of the Wharf Management Office, the Deputy Commander of the Water Police, and Chief Guan of the 1st District of the Public Security Bureau. Antai Company's Changtai Ship Encounters Danger and Returns to Shanghai

The Antai Shipping Company's Changtai ship has always sailed between Xinghua and Quanzhou in Fujian, transporting flour and other items to Fujian, and bringing longan to Shanghai. This time, it set sail from Shanghai and exited the port on the morning of the 5th of this month. At 6:10 pm on the 8th, the ship arrived at the sea near Passaga Island and encountered a strong storm. The captain, seeing the opportunity, immediately directed the ship to face the waves and ran at full power to resist the storm. At 6:30 pm, the ship ran aground in that area and struck a hidden reef, and the bottom of the hold was broken by the reef, allowing seawater to enter. The captain assessed the situation and found that there was no major problem, so he ordered the driver to sail to the nearby sea. On the morning of the 9th, the ship arrived at the fallen island and immediately anchored, grounding the ship on the sand. It sent a telegram to Shanghai for help and temporarily repaired the damaged area before sailing back to Shanghai. It anchored on the Yangshupu side of the riverbank, and the company rushed to repair the damaged bottom of the ship. It also submitted a request to the Maritime Affairs Bureau to send personnel to inspect the ship. The ship has a load capacity of 2,000 tons, and this time it was loaded with more than 1,900 tons of flour and general merchandise. Those in the bottom of the ship have been damaged by water. According to people in the company, there was not much damage from the Changtai's accident. It is now scheduled to sail from Shanghai to Xinghua and Quanzhou as usual on the 21st.

The Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways Administration issued a notice to various departments yesterday, stating: "According to the report submitted by the Two-Railways Promoting Domestic Goods Movement Committee, it is the national duty of citizens to purchase domestic goods. The most formidable enemy that devastates domestic goods is foreign goods, especially Japanese goods, which account for the largest proportion of foreign goods. Everyone knows this. The ship has a displacement of 700 tons, is 200 feet long, 20 feet wide, and has a draft of 10 feet 6 inches. It has two 3-pound guns in the front and rear, 12 machine guns, and two speedboats. The equipment is very complete. The third warship, Hexing, is also scheduled to be completed next month and delivered to the Customs for use.

New Fujian Civil Affairs Director Li Zuyu Discusses Policy Guidelines

Focus on Rectifying Officialdom and Unifying Powers

Scheduled to Take the Changsha Maru to Fujian Tomorrow

The newly appointed member of the Fujian Provincial Government and Director of Civil Affairs, Li Zuyu, was originally a lawyer in Shanghai. Since accepting the appointment, he has been busy ending his legal affairs. Because of the repeated urgings of Fujian Chairman Chen Yi, he is scheduled to take the Changsha Maru to Fujian tomorrow (19th) to take office. A reporter from the Xin Xin News Agency paid a special visit yesterday, and the conversation on various issues is as follows:

Rectifying Officialdom

Li said first that he holds a kind of determination and sacrifice to serve as the Director of Civil Affairs in Fujian Province, that is, to seek benefits for the country and the people, not to seek personal fame and wealth. He believes that there are many aspects of civil affairs that should be improved, but it is necessary to start with the rectification of officialdom.

Prioritizing Assessment

Regarding the rectification of officialdom, Li takes three points: First, after taking office, he will prioritize the assessment and appointment of talents in the province (referring to Fujian Province) who do not violate the personnel standards expressed by Chairman Chen (Yi), and hope that the number of people from this province who are employed can exceed those from outside the province.

Unifying Powers

Second, it is heard that the power of personnel administration in Fujian Province cannot be unified. If it is not rectified, it will be a major obstacle to officialdom. After taking office, he plans to first rectify it. The length of his tenure in Fujian depends on whether the proposed rectification and unification work can proceed.

Personnel Standards

Third, Fujian Province is a poor province, so he hopes that all officials in Fujian, large and small, can be frugal, hardworking, responsible, and have a spirit of sacrifice, so that they can alleviate the suffering of the people of Fujian. This is the standard of personnel he limits, so all those who are accustomed to extravagance, or whose words and deeds do not match, are on the list of those who will be dismissed.

Overseas Chinese Investment

The Xin Xin News Agency reporter asked what his opinion was on the fact that the Fujian Overseas Chinese Association in Shanghai, the Overseas Chinese Federation, and the Overseas Fujian Save Hometown Association and other organizations had previously submitted a request to the Executive Yuan and the Military Commission to plan the ten coastal counties of southern Fujian for overseas Chinese to transfer funds back to the country for construction and to try out local self-government. Li said that he did not know the details of this point, but it depended on how Chairman Chen (Yi) of Fujian Province decided. The Fujian Provincial Government will welcome overseas Chinese to transfer back to the country for construction.

Guo Chengen and Others Establish a Gas Production Company

Someone Attempts to Sabotage

According to the Hua Dong News Agency, there were only two companies in Shanghai that manufactured and sold industrial oxygen and carbon dioxide: the French-owned Oriental Company and the British-owned Oxygen Company. Therefore, they had a monopoly and engaged in speculation and hoarding, and Chinese factories have suffered from this for more than a day. The amount of money leaked out every year is also quite alarming. Guo Chengen, the former director of the Central Mint, and others, aware of this suffering, took promoting domestic goods as a prerequisite and gathered like-minded people to purchase land and build houses at 537 Liaoyang Road, establishing the China Industrial Gas Production Co., Ltd. They hired Li Yunxian as the manager and planned for several years before starting to produce oxygen, carbon dioxide, and other types of gas in December last year. The oxygen composition has been certified by chemical inspection agencies to reach 99.8 degrees, which can save more than 50% of consumption compared to ordinary 94-96 degree goods. The carbon dioxide composition is also very pure. Now, Chinese factories in Shanghai, such as the Yabuer Electric Factory, are purchasing them one after another. Even foreign-owned businesses, such as the Electric Power Company, the Waterworks Company, and the Old Shipyard, who used to purchase from British and French companies, have also changed to ordering from this company. As the company's purpose is to promote domestic goods, not to make profits, the prices are lower than those of the British and French companies. Recently, in order to maintain their business, the two companies have had to lower prices from time to time. Recently, they have used their economic aggression tactics, deliberately depressing prices in an attempt to squeeze them out. The company has maintained its composure, refused to yield, and fought to the end, and the foreign merchants could do nothing. Unexpectedly, the police recently arrested a suspicious person near the company. According to the person, he was sent by someone to take secret actions in front of the company's factory, hoping to harm it secretly. Manager Li thought that since the case had been discovered first and there had been no tangible losses, he was magnanimous and did not pursue it further. Unexpectedly, on the night of the following day, someone threw a bomb at the company, intending to destroy it. Fortunately, it did not explode, and there was no loss. The company has now reported the matter to the police and requested an investigation.

Nanshi Concession Telephone Trunk Lines Being Replaced with Armored Cables

For Safety, Work Started Yesterday

Total of 200 Pairs to be Completed in Two Weeks

The Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Transportation, in view of the fact that the lines connecting Nanshi to the Concession used to be overhead cables, has decided, for safety's sake, to replace the overhead cables on the telephone poles along Min Guo Road from Xiaodongmen to the Jixiang Street intersection with armored cables buried underground. A total of 200 pairs will be installed, divided into two lines, each with 100 pairs. It is understood that these are the trunk lines from Nanshi to the Concession and from the Concession to Nanshi. Yesterday, the bureau sent engineers and workers to start digging, and the armored cables are scheduled to be laid on Monday. It is estimated that the work will be completed in two weeks.

Gunshots Break the Early Morning Silence - A Wounded Robber Apprehended

Three Robbers Suddenly Invade Yuan Futang’s Home Yesterday Morning

Two Detectives Pursue After Receiving Report, Gunfire Heard All the Way

丨Rickshaw Puller Bravely Captures Robber, Wounded by Robber's Gun丨

At about 8:00 AM yesterday morning, a robbery and resisting arrest incident involving gunfire occurred on Rue Bayle and Avenue Dubail in the French Concession. As a result, one robber was shot and captured, and a rickshaw puller was severely wounded by the robber. Details are recorded below.

Three Robbers Arrive Suddenly in the Early Morning

Yuan Futang, a native of Shandong, is 62 years old and has been running the Hengxiang Tong Customs Brokerage at No. 4, Lane 135, Jiangxi Road, Public Concession, as the manager for many years. His business is quite prosperous. He lives at No. 44, Xingye Li, Avenue Dubail, French Concession. Yesterday morning, being the fourth day of the Lunar New Year, Yuan had already gone to his office. Only his nephew Yuan Shenchu (38 years old) and a female servant were guarding the door at home, while Yuan's wife and two children were still asleep in bed. Suddenly, three robbers arrived.

Entering the Bedroom to Rob

At 8:45 AM, the three robbers broke in through the front door. One robber remained at the front door to keep watch, while the other two, one wearing a scarlet Western suit and the other an overcoat, speaking with Xiang-E (Hunan-Hubei) accents and carrying guns, barged straight into Yuan's wife's bedroom on the second floor. Yuan's wife was terrified. The robbers slapped the female servant several times on the face, forcing her to reveal where the money was hidden. As a result, they robbed 46 silver dollars in cash, one gold ring, and one gold ear pick. While the two robbers were searching, a neighbor surnamed Yu noticed what was happening and immediately secretly reported it to the Lane Inspector, who then reported it to Chinese Constable No. 471.

Two Detectives Give Chase with Whistles

After the two robbers had finished looting, they rushed out of the door and fled eastwards along Rue Lafayette. The two detectives followed closely behind, blowing their whistles as they pursued. Knowing that things were not going well, the two robbers fled along Rue Muling, turned south into Rue Pére Robert, and ran frantically, hoping to escape.

Rickshaw Puller Injured While Capturing Robber

At that time, a rickshaw puller named Zhu Afu was resting at the corner of Rue Bayle. Seeing the robbers running towards him, Zhu bravely stepped forward, intending to capture them head-on. Seeing this, the robber in the Western suit fired at Zhu, who fell to the ground. The robbers continued to flee until they reached the entrance of Hengchang Li. By this time, the two detectives had caught up, and the two sides exchanged fire. Gunshots rang out like a string of pearls.

One Robber Wounded and Captured

Unexpectedly, a resident of No. 18, Hengchang Li, was Chen Jinfan, Detective Sergeant No. 121 of the French Police. At the time, Detective Chen had just gotten up to eat when he suddenly heard gunshots. At first, he suspected it was children playing with firecrackers for the New Year, but when he heard police whistles, he knew something was wrong. He quickly grabbed his gun and rushed out, only to see one robber lying in a pool of blood, having been shot. He arrested the robber, who had been shot in the abdomen and left heel. At the same time, Chief Inspector Jin Jiulin had heard the news and arrived. He first sent the wounded robber to Guangci Hospital and questioned him briefly. The robber claimed his surname was Wang, but his answers were vague. The chief inspector immediately reported to the police chief to apprehend the remaining accomplices for further investigation.

Qiu Tianbao's Storekeeper Surrenders, Reporting Embezzlement

Embezzled Total of 120 Taels of Gold Worth 14,000 Yuan

Fearing Trouble for Guarantor, He Surrenders to Zhabei Police Station with Lawyer

Xu Kaitai, a native of Ningbo, living at No. 82, Hengji Li, Gordon Road, was a storekeeper at the Qiu Tianbao Silver Store at No. 500, Nanjing Road. Yesterday afternoon at 6:30 PM, Xu, accompanied by a lawyer, surrendered to the Zhabei Police Station, stating that due to speculation, he had embezzled 120 taels of gold from the store, worth 14,000 yuan. Fearing that his guarantor would be implicated, he surrendered. After investigation by Chinese Detective Zhang Yuanqing and Detective Wan Wangke, it was learned that Xu had been a storekeeper at Qiu Tianbao since 1926. Because of his good character, he had gained the trust of the manager. Later, his younger brother, Kai Fu, had embezzled more than 1,000 yuan from the Qinghua Silver Store. Due to sibling ties, Xu helped to make up for it. He secretly took goods from the store to repay the debt. He then planned to speculate in mark (biao jin), but repeatedly failed, resulting in such a large debt. Recently, due to the change in the system of weights and measures, the store wanted to check the inventory. Fearing exposure, Xu reported to Assistant Manager Yao Guiqing. However, Yao did not report it to the police but only negotiated compensation with Xu's guarantor. Fearing trouble for his guarantor, Xu went to the police station to report it. Xu was immediately detained and sent to the First Special District Court, Criminal Division One, yesterday morning. The police lawyer Li Zhishan charged him with embezzlement in the course of business under Article 357, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law. However, since it was a voluntary surrender, he requested that the penalty be determined in accordance with the regulations on voluntary surrender. Xu Kaitai confessed to the above situation without denial, requesting leniency, and claimed that he would find ways to repay the embezzled funds within his ability. Judge Qian Hongye verified the confession, ordered the conclusion of the arguments, and scheduled the verdict for Saturday morning next week. Xu Kaitai was allowed to be released on bail of 2,000 yuan.

Ministry of Transportation Sends Shen Jiyun to Wuhan to Adjudicate the Wanxiang Disaster

One Trial Has Already Been Held in Wuhan

Responsibility Issues Becoming Clearer

The case of the Sanbei Company's Wanxiang steamer colliding with and sinking the Yunbing Chai wheelship Luan, which was carrying soldiers, on the Qichun Diaoyu River on December 10 of last year, resulting in the drowning of more than 300 recruits, was reported in this newspaper earlier. The Hankou Navigation Administration Bureau has now organized a Ship Collision Committee, hired navigation experts, and is holding an adjudication. The latest news is as follows.

Headquarters Conducts Thorough Investigation

After the Wanxiang collided with and sank the Luan wheelship, Wang Jingkui, the head of the Wuhan Fourth Recruitment Office, sent a telegram to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek stating that the Luan was carrying more than 200 recruits to Jiangxi. On the evening of November 11, while sailing on the Qichun Diaoyu River, it was struck by the Sanbei's Wanxiang steamer, which was sailing upstream against the waves. At that time, it was dusk, and both sides sounded their horns as a warning. When they got close, the Wanxiang wrongly shifted course, causing the Luan to be unable to avoid it in time, resulting in a collision and sinking. The Wanxiang stopped its engines to rescue, but other than rescuing more than 40 people, more than 300 people were buried in the belly of the fish. In addition to investigating and reporting the names, martial arts, and clothing of the drowned recruits, he was first telegraphing a report. After receiving the report, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek immediately sent Wang Wu, an inspector from the headquarters, to the scene of the accident and to ports such as Hankou to conduct an on-site investigation. Wang Wu's report was largely the same as that reported by Wang Jingkui. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, considering that this case involved the drowning of more than 200 lives, and that the responsibility lay with which party, ordered the Jiangxi-Anhui-Henan Bandit Suppression Headquarters to send personnel to conduct a thorough investigation to clarify the truth.

Three Trials

Regarding the issue of responsibility in this case, the pilots of the Sanbei Wanxiang steamer and the Luan wheelship blamed each other, each with their own reasons, and both claimed to have sounded their whistles before the collision. The two sides could not reach a decision, so the Bandit Suppression Headquarters, together with the Hankou Navigation Administration Bureau, notified Sanbei and Luan steamer owners to hire impartial personnel from the shipping industry to go to Wuhan to form a Collision Arbitration Committee. The Sanbei side appointed Wang Youshi, captain of the Jianguo ship of the local China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, as its arbitration representative. After Wang Youshi arrived in Wuhan, the first step was to conduct several on-site investigations in Qichun with all relevant personnel, collecting witness statements and special evidence for the case. He then summoned the ship owners and pilots of the Wanxiang and Luan steamers to the Hankou Navigation Administration Bureau to review the sailing history of both sides and to investigate the circumstances of the collision of the two ships. From the beginning of January this year to the present, the crew members of the two ships have been summoned for three trials. Both sides had their own arguments, and there were initial clues as to responsibility. However, for the sake of careful arbitration, another trial is needed before a judgment can be made.

Ministry Sends Special Commissioner

This case is a rare tragedy among domestic merchant ship disasters on the Yangtze River in recent years, and the victims were armed comrades who lost more than 300 lives. It was feared that relying solely on the arbitrators of the two sides would not be credible. Therefore, after the Hankou Navigation Administration Bureau reported to the Ministry of Transportation, Minister Zhu Jiahua decided to send an additional arbitrator from the Ministry to Wuhan to participate in the trial, but this person must be highly respected in the navigation industry and have excellent academic knowledge in order to be competent for this important task. After considering the matter, Minister Zhu decided to send Shen Jiyun, the current Chief Shipmaster of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, to serve as the special commissioner appointed by the Ministry of Transportation to participate in the arbitration. After the decision was made, the commission was issued to Shanghai, and Mr. Shen immediately went to Wuhan to join the arbitration court as the chief arbitrator to try this unprecedented shipwreck disaster.

Wang Lao Jiu Asks Wife to Remarry

Yao Zhifa Has Nothing More to Say

Tea House Card Game Leads to Grudge and Knife Attack

Wang A'siu Bets But Doesn't Get Matched

Next Day He is Slashed by a Crowd

Wang A'siu, 30 years old, a native of Suzhou, is a fruit peddler living at No. 2, Delian Li, Baliliqiao Street, French Concession. As it was the beginning of the Lunar New Year, he was bored at home and went to the Dexing Tea House in Baxianqiao every day to drink tea and pass the time. The afternoon before yesterday, A'siu went to the tea house and saw that a large game of pai gow (Chinese dominoes) was being played in the middle of the tea room, with loud shouts and excitement. A'siu was tempted and also went to place a bet. At that time, the banker was losing badly, so those who bet money were all very happy. However, when A'siu bet six jiao (cents), he was not matched due to the confusion. He negotiated with the banker, but the banker refused to admit it. The two sides argued, almost resorting to violence. Fortunately, others persuaded them to stop. Yesterday afternoon at 3:50 PM, A'siu went to the tea house again. Before he could sit down, eight or nine men rushed up from downstairs, holding sharp knives. When they saw A'siu, they started arguing about the previous night's incident. Before they could say a few words, they slashed A'siu with their knives. A'siu was unable to dodge and had the tip of his left index finger cut off. His left leg, left knee, and back were also each slashed once, and he fell to the ground with severe injuries, bleeding profusely. The tea drinkers nearby were terrified and fled downstairs. Fortunately, nearby Annamite (Vietnamese) constables learned of the incident, went upstairs, arrested three of the assailants, and took them to the police station for interrogation. Wang A'siu was rushed to Renji Hospital for treatment.

Fang Junqian Accuses Sun Hengfu of Embezzlement

Initial Trial Dismissed

Second Appeal Rejected

Sun Hengfu, the president of the Siming Bank, was accused by Fang Junqian, a shareholder of the bank, of engaging in embezzlement and harming the interests of the shareholders. Last winter, Fang, through a lawyer, filed a criminal self-suit against Sun with the First Special District Court, stating that the defendant had fabricated and altered account books, with malicious intentions and extremely dangerous methods. Among the most obvious, there were many discrepancies between the annual business report and the diary table for the 20th year. The plaintiff had obtained solid evidence of the defendant's wrongdoing and could prove it item by item. The defendant's actions were unforgivable by both law and morality, so he filed the self-suit, requesting that the case be investigated and punished according to the law. After receiving the complaint, the court held that a shareholder's accusation against a manager, according to the Limited Company Regulations, must be jointly signed by one-tenth of all shareholders to be legal, and that the plaintiff was only suing individually, which seemed inappropriate. Therefore, only the plaintiff was summoned to court to ask about the reasons for the lawsuit. Although the plaintiff's lawyer stated that the plaintiff's accusation against Sun Hengfu was a personal act and did not involve the entire company, and therefore did not need to consider the company's regulations, the judge ultimately determined that the plaintiff had no right to sue and ruled that the case would not be accepted. However, after receiving the court's ruling, Fang Junqian was very dissatisfied and entrusted the original lawyer to submit a petition to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, appealing the initial trial decision, and stating the reasons why the plaintiff had the right to file a criminal self-suit against Sun Hengfu, requesting that the original ruling be overturned and an appropriate ruling be made to correct the situation. It is now known that after receiving the petition, the Second Branch of the High Court requested the case files from the Special Court. After deliberation by Court President Yu Chan and the court's judges, it was decided to uphold the original ruling and dismiss the appeal. However, after hearing the news, the plaintiff still expressed dissatisfaction.

Thirty-Year Typing Expert Testifies That Check Font in Major Fraud Case

All from Typewriters Belonging to Englishman Mackintosh

Each Typewriter Letter has Special Characteristics, None are the Same

In the case of the embezzlement of large sums from the Chartered Bank of India, Australia and China, in addition to the two Russians and three Chinese who have been convicted by the First Special District Court, the Englishman Mackintosh, the Portuguese Baptista, and a Frenchman are still on trial. Englishman Mackintosh recently appeared before the British Consular Police Court, where Viedt, a typing expert with thirty years of experience, testified that many documents related to the case came from the machine No. 18715 taken by the police from the defendant's firm, and that one of the digits of the fake check of 188,000 yuan, and one digit of the fake check of 136,688 yuan and 25 jiao (cents), all came from machine No. 1,637,792 in the defendant's office. This machine was also seized by the police. He also claimed that the letters on typewriters each have special characteristics, none are the same, and that any expert can distinguish them without error. The defendant's lawyer then cross-examined him, but Viedt remained steadfast in his testimony. Chief Inspector York of the police then gave a detailed account of his several meetings with the defendant. As it was getting late, the magistrate adjourned the hearing to Tuesday next week. The Portuguese Baptista was also tried by Portuguese Consul-General Xavier, but the details were not known as the hearing was not public. It is only known that the two Russians and three Chinese who had already been convicted by the First Special District Court were summoned to court that day, and then the trial was indefinitely postponed to allow other witnesses to be summoned for questioning.

This will allow the business to continue, and it may be able to open as usual this day in Yue Road. Because the shareholder Huang Zhenrong's side still needs to be dealt with, it is still being reorganized. It is estimated that it will be completed and realized in the near future.

Luckily Rescued and Reborn

Major Clash in Dachang Militia Due to Misunderstanding

More Than 100 Shots Fired by Both Sides

Cause Was a Bride Snatching

Yan Quansheng, a coach of the Eighth Jia of the Dachang Town Militia in Baoshan County, had previously been betrothed to the Zhu family of Kangjiazhai, about three li northeast of the town. After entering the family, he left without marrying due to certain reasons. Both the man and the woman have now grown up, the woman being 28 years old this year. The family consists of only an old mother and daughter who live together. On the evening of the 13th of this month, at around 7:00 PM, Yan led more than 20 militiamen to the Zhu family to snatch the bride. They had already snatched Miss Zhu and traveled less than half a li when the villagers of Kangjiazhai heard about it and sounded the alarm with gongs. The surrounding villages, such as Wujiazhuang and Lijialou, suddenly heard the sound of gongs and mistook it for a robbery. In an instant, gongs were sounded everywhere, and the militiamen chased after them. Both sides opened fire, and the sound of gunfire was heard far and wide. The fighting intensified. After about half an hour, the two sides fired hundreds of shots. As a result, Yan was outnumbered and was caught by the Kangjiazhai Militia, who seized Miss Zhu and captured four of Yan Quansheng's militiamen, including Yan Jinsheng. Zhu was outnumbered and retreated. It is now known that the local gentry, Mr. Wang Yingshi, is currently being asked to mediate. Yesterday afternoon, the reporter went to Mr. Wang's residence to inquire. According to his answer, the plan is to first dismiss Coach Yan and fine him ten street lights as a warning and to enforce discipline. According to local villagers, there have been several robberies since last August, and a man named Dai Xiaoheshang was shot and killed by bandits. Therefore, when the villagers hear the sound of gongs, they must rush out to pursue and arrest them.

Lawyer Zhan Jifeng's Home Robbed

At 7 PM the other night, the residence of the renowned lawyer Zhan Jifeng, located in the Datong Li on Baike Road, was suddenly entered by six bandits who gained entry under false pretenses. They first went to the downstairs side room, produced handguns, and intimidated Zhan's two secretaries, ordering them to remain silent. The secretaries initially refused to yield, resulting in a violent assault. They had no choice but to endure without resistance. The bandits then proceeded upstairs directly to the inner chambers. At that time, Mr. Zhan and his family were out on business. The bandits then ransacked the cabinets and chests at will, engaging in unrestrained looting. Although Zhan had been practicing law in Shanghai for many years, the cost of living in the city was very high, and he barely had enough for sustenance, with little savings. The bandits searched until past 8 PM, but still did not find any valuable items. However, unwilling to have made the trip in vain, they grabbed several legal documents from Zhan's office before fleeing. When Zhan returned home and checked his belongings, he realized that what had been stolen were documents related to cases transferred by the Public Security Bureau to the concession courts. This was because Mr. Zhan also served as a legal advisor to the municipal Public Security Bureau. Zhan has since reported the incident to the relevant police station, requesting an investigation.

Wen Zongyao's Concubine Case Continues Hearing

Most witnesses appeared in court to testify

The court ordered the conclusion of the debate and scheduled sentencing for the 19th

Wen Zongyao, who once served as one of the seven Southwest Chief Executives, was sued by Yu Wang, a widow from Hangzhou claiming to be the mother of Jin Yuan (now renamed Shouzhen), for abduction of a minor because Wen took Jin Yuan, a former prostitute, as his concubine. The First Special District Court summoned Wen to appear in court for interrogation. The details have been reported in previous issues. Yesterday afternoon, presiding Judge Wu Zehan held a continued hearing. The plaintiff, Yu Wang and her daughter, claimed illness and did not appear. The plaintiff's lawyer requested a postponement, but the defendant opposed the postponement, arguing that the witnesses had all arrived. After arguments from both sides' lawyers, the court decided to proceed. Tao Rubo, a detective from the Xinzha Police Station, testified that Wen Zongyao reported the escape of his concubine Shouzhen on February 1. He was dispatched to investigate the situation at 584 Da Tong Road and 25 De'an Lane on North Shanxi Road. Next, Chen Wang, a landlady from Da Tong Road, testified that Wen Zongyao rented a three-story loft from her for 15 yuan per month. After the rental was completed, he moved in with Shouzhen. However, Wen only came to the house during the day and never stayed overnight. His concubine initially stayed at home, but on the 25th of the previous month, she suddenly left with a female servant and a trunk of luggage, saying that she was going to the hospital for childbirth. Lao Liu, a former prostitute at 25 De'an Lane, testified that Shouzhen's original name was Jin Yuan, born to the sister of Wang Yang. When the sister died, Jin Yuan was only eight years old, so she was raised by Wang Yang and never knew that she had a biological mother. Two years ago, when Jin Yuan was 24 years old, a Northerner wanted to marry her, but Jin Yuan refused. Later, Wen took her as his concubine, and Wang Yang received a dowry of 1,200 yuan. Zhao Ruixin, who had frequented that brothel, testified that he had visited De'an Lane in 1924 and 1927 and had met Wen there. At that time, Jin Yuan was still young. Finally, the lawyers for both sides mutually debated the original arguments to conclusion. Judge Wu announced that the verdict would be announced on the 19th.

Construction Factory Owner Ling Songting Sued for Abuse by Concubine

Ling Songting, the 54-year-old owner of a construction factory located at 135 Route Masnan, French Concession, and a native of Nanhui County, Pudong, has been doing well in business in recent years and has accumulated considerable savings. As a result, he has three wives and concubines at home. Last year, he took a woman from a brothel as his fourth concubine. After the fourth concubine entered the house, Ling began to abuse his third concubine, Cai Jinbao (29 years old, native of Pudong). Because of this, Cai could not bear to live with him and returned to her mother's home. She hired a lawyer to file a complaint with the Criminal Division of the Second Special Court, accusing Ling of abandonment and demanding 5,000 yuan in private compensation. She was summoned yesterday afternoon. According to Cai Jinbao, she married Ling as a concubine when she was 19 years old. After entering the house, they lived in harmony. Unexpectedly, after Ling married a prostitute as his fourth concubine last year, he became hostile to her, deprived her of food and necessities, and frequently abused her. On July 23 of last year, he not only beat her but also destroyed the bed, curtains, and clothes in the room. The situation became unbearable, so she returned to her mother's home and requested an investigation and compensation for her to live in a nunnery and cultivate her mind in peace. Ling Songting testified that he treated his wives and concubines equally and did not abuse the plaintiff. He also said the second concubine, Lu Yuezhen, was a witness to his claims. An officer commanded Lu Yuezhen to appear in court, and Lu Yuezhen, age 50, testified that she lived with the plaintiff and others. Last year, the plaintiff and the fourth concubine had a quarrel, so her husband got angry and broke a glass window, but he did not beat the plaintiff. As for the women, each received 5 yuan per month for personal use. Recently, her husband's business has been slow, so he has not paid them, which is true. The officer asked the plaintiff if she had any witnesses to the abuse and abandonment by her husband, and Cai replied that she did not. When asked if she was willing to return home with her husband, she replied that she had been abused and did not want to return. The plaintiff's lawyer claimed that the defendant had abused and abandoned the plaintiff since marrying his fourth concubine. The plaintiff is lame and completely unable to support herself. The defendant has committed the crime of abandonment under Article 309 of the Criminal Code. The lawyer requested an investigation and compensation. The defendant's lawyer also made a defense. Judge Xiong ruled that the debate was over and declared Ling Songting not guilty and dismissed the plaintiff's private lawsuit.

Due to mediation by relatives and friends, a request was made to withdraw the case.

The police lawyer said that further research was needed.

The Tongchang Oil Factory at No. 80 Route de la Grande Armée formerly employed Zhu Bingsheng from Shanghai as an accountant. Unexpectedly, during the past year, Zhu misappropriated 5,419 yuan of public funds for his own use. It was important to study whether this case fell under the category of cases that could only be prosecuted upon complaint, according to the Criminal Code. Cao Baogen Commits Suicide in a Hotel

Cao Baogen, a 24-year-old local man, lived in a bungalow at No. 16 Nankai Road, Caojiadu, West Shanghai. He used to work as a road worker but had been unemployed for a long time due to rheumatic fever and was struggling to make a living. On the 16th (the other day), he checked into the Yong'an Inn in the Chengda Alley on Xintiantong Road. After dinner, he secretly took a lethal dose of something that produced smoke and committed suicide behind everyone's back. Recently, the weather has been warm, and many people in the Nanshi and Chenghuang areas have contracted smallpox. Sun Guochang (26 years old), a native of Anhui, lived in the rear building at No. 56 Hunan Railway Station Road. He worked to earn a living and had no relatives in Shanghai. Provisional Regulations for Pilotage Management

Since the authority to manage pilotage at various seaports was returned to the control of our government, all pilotage affairs rights stipulated in 1868 have now been inherited by the Shanghai Pilotage Management Committee. The selection of committee members has been reported in previous issues. It is now learned that the Committee, in accordance with the Provisional Regulations for Pilotage Management promulgated by the National Government, has resolved the meeting rules and detailed rules of procedure, which have been submitted to the National Government for approval and promulgation. The original text is recorded as follows:

Meeting Rules

Article 1: The Committee's meetings shall be organized in accordance with the provisions of Article 2 of the Provisional Regulations for Pilotage Management. Article 2: Committee meetings must have at least five members present, and a majority vote of the members shall be required for passage. Article 3: The powers and duties of the Committee's meetings are as follows: (1) Matters stipulated in the Provisional Regulations for Pilotage Management; (2) Matters concerning the appointment of experienced professionals to participate in the examination of pilot qualifications; (3) Matters concerning the recovery of the Pilot Association's property and compensation for its value; (4) Matters concerning the determination of the salaries of pilots in various districts; (5) Matters concerning the formulation of the terms of service of foreign pilots; (6) Matters concerning the review of proposals submitted by various members; (7) Matters concerning the review of the Committee's revenue and expenditure; (8) Matters concerning the appointment and evaluation of the Committee's staff; (9) Other important matters. Article 4: The Committee's meetings shall be held once a month for regular meetings. Extraordinary meetings may be convened in case of urgent matters. Article 5: If there are any matters not covered by these rules, they may be amended by a two-thirds vote of the members present at the Committee's meetings. Article 6: These rules shall be implemented upon approval.

Detailed Rules of Procedure

Article 1: These detailed rules are formulated in accordance with the duties and responsibilities stipulated in the Provisional Regulations for Pilotage Management. Article 2: Important matters of the Committee, except for matters not stipulated in the Provisional Regulations for Pilotage Management, shall be handled by the Committee's meetings after deliberation and decision, after requesting instructions. Article 3: Members of the Committee may at any time submit proposals for improving pilotage affairs to the meeting for discussion and suggestion to the relevant departments. Article 4: Personnel appointed by the Committee shall be appointed in the name of the Committee and reported to the Ministry of Finance for record. Article 5: The Committee shall have a Director of the Secretariat, who shall be concurrently appointed by one of the representatives of the relevant central departments, and shall also have one Chinese and one English secretary, and a number of clerks, to manage the Committee's meeting records and documents, accounting, general affairs, and licenses. The method of task allocation shall be determined separately. Article 6: The Committee shall have a Director of the Business Office, who shall be concurrently appointed by the Harbor Master, and shall also have a number of clerks, to manage the scheduling of pilotage services, the calculation and collection of pilotage fees, the inspection of pilot licenses, etc. The method of task allocation shall be determined separately. Article 7: The minutes of the Committee's meetings shall be read by the Chairman at the next meeting, and after each member confirms that they are correct, they shall be signed by the Chairman. Article 8: If there are any matters not covered by these detailed rules, they may be amended by the Committee's meetings. Article 9: These detailed rules shall be implemented upon approval.

Incoming Items

Modern Cold Leg Disease

(2) Zhai Shaoheng

Prevention of Cold Legs: We already know that cold legs are caused by the legs being exposed to cold. Therefore, the way to prevent it is simply to keep the legs warm and protect them from the cold. As for whether it looks good or not, fashionable or not, of course, we cannot care about that. However, as long as everyone dresses like this, it won't look bad. Now, I want to first talk about a few things that I can think of:

(1) When going out, shoes and socks should be thick, and the soles of the shoes should preferably be made of felt to prevent cold air from entering the soles of the feet. The trouser legs should be long, and it is best to install a section of elasticated gaiters inside the trousers to prevent the icy northwest wind from blowing straight into the trousers. According to the current general dress, wearing a velvet hat on the head, a leather coat on the body, short silk trousers on the lower body, and thin silk stockings and leather sandals on the feet, it is okay for those who get in and out of cars, but those who take rickshaws will be exposed to the northwest wind, which blows directly on their feet and into their trousers. Even a hot water bottle the size of a fist may not be able to withstand this ruthless cold.

(2) When attending class, schools with good buildings and sufficient funds naturally have floors, cement floors, and radiators, which are very comfortable. However, in general poor schools, the doors and windows are closed but drafty, the stove is there but has no fire, and the ground is damp and made of mud bricks. Being in such a place, sitting from 8:00 in the morning to 5:00 in the afternoon every day, winter after winter, year after year, I am afraid that many people will develop cold legs. Therefore, people studying in poor schools should be prepared to go out and sit in the open air, so as to reduce the harm of being exposed to cold on the legs.

(3) When playing cards, there is no problem in wealthy people's homes. In ordinary people's homes, especially on damp mud bricks, several small benches should always be placed under the table for the card players to rest their feet on. If not, then playing sixteen or twenty-four rounds day and night, until after midnight, when it is almost dawn, you will feel numb hands and cold feet, and a stiff back. This may not be a big problem for a day or two, but if it goes on for years, it will definitely lead to cold legs.

(4) When watching opera and movies, there is of course no problem in fancy theaters. Moreover, fashionable young mistresses and young ladies only watch the last one or two acts of the opera, so the time is not long and the harm is less. However, those opera fans who want to watch from the opening act to the old female character doing the wedding ceremony must wear more clothes on their lower body, because watching opera also involves sitting still. And the equipment of the theaters is ultimately incomplete. If you sit in a drafty place for a long time, it will also be bad. Also, I recently had an experience that is also worth noting. That is, in the summer of the 22nd year of the Republic of China, I accidentally went to a certain big theater with my family to watch a movie. I don't need to say that a certain big theater is a fancy theater that everyone knows. Sitting inside, you can forget that it is summer, because there is air conditioning inside. Who knew that I, who had not enjoyed this kind of comfort, felt cold air reaching my waist from my feet in less than half an hour, so my waist hurt, and my stomach hurt. Because I didn't want to spoil the fun of the group, I reluctantly persevered to the end, but I was in great pain. Later, I went there again, and I got the same result again. So I made up my mind not to set foot there again. When I told others about it, many people had the same illness as me. I think people with the same illness and women during menstruation and after childbirth should at least pay attention. (To be continued)

Reading Q&A

On Current Writing

(2)

We greatly value your self-study experience. You are using the correct methods for learning to write and collecting vocabulary. (When you get good phrases, you hide them away), (for more than a year) (you have accumulated quite a few newspaper scraps), and then (cut out the words that please you)

, (paste them in a notebook). Naturally, in your environment, it is already quite commendable that you can do this with such care.

As for your lack of understanding of modern writing, it is no wonder, your environment really does not allow you to have much access to (writing). However, we don't think it's a pity for you, because being a person doesn't necessarily mean you have to be good at writing. There are many people with good writing skills who don't understand the ways of the world. I think striving for success in writing is simply unnecessary; but if you learn modern Chinese language to understand (reality), that is a meaningful and necessary thing.

Modern Chinese language undoubtedly has what you said (some classical Chinese mixed with (le) (de) (ma); and colloquial Chinese sometimes inserts classical Chinese words.) In principle, this cannot be said to be bad. The Chinese language is currently in an era of transformation. It needs to expand its new vocabulary, so there is nothing wrong with colloquial Chinese containing classical Chinese words, as long as it is a living reference. As for adding colloquial Chinese to classical Chinese, this proves the decline of classical Chinese. It must maintain the old style and old words, which can never exist and be popular. However, in the current types of writing, there are already many purely beautiful colloquial writings, and colloquial writing has long been firmly established in China.

(Every sentence in the colloquial style seems to be broken up, even every word cannot be put down.) This is probably because you are too deeply influenced by classical Chinese and are not very close to colloquial Chinese, otherwise, you are indeed reading the worst works.

In modern colloquial Chinese, there are two types of writing that are more difficult to read. The first type is divided into two types: one is writing that implies more than it says, or so-called (humorous) writing, (such as the works of Lin Yutang, Lu Xun, etc.), and the other is meticulously descriptive writing; (such as the works of Xu Zhimo, etc.). The other type is translated writing.

The (difficulty) of the former is not only in the writing, but also in whether your emotions can understand the lofty emotions contained in a work of art, and whether it can arouse resonance? The latter also requires your academic ability, whether you are completely unfamiliar with the content contained in a certain work? Or do you have some foundation? So you can't misunderstand that you don't understand the writing because you don't understand the theory! However, we also know that there are indeed some (incomprehensible), (stiff), (too Europeanized) problems in the current translations. This is partly because the translator's ability is too low, and partly because of the shortcomings of the Chinese language itself. In short, this is a temporary phenomenon, which can be avoided after the end of the future language reform. We cannot oppose (foreign words), (foreign styles), (precise long sentence structure) because there are a few difficult-to-read translations!

(Which one is the standard), but it cannot be determined. But for beginners, it is still best to start with pure colloquial language. If you must point out a (typical) one, I think Guo Moruo's prose is the most fluent type in colloquial language. You can find one of his prose collections to read!

The piece of writing you attached is a rather simple essay. There are many such writings now. You can go to our book catalog to find (essays) (modern literary collections) books, which are guaranteed to satisfy your interest.

Finally, what I want to remind you in particular is: you don't have to seek success in writing, you should take learning modern writing as a means of studying other subjects. (Please refer to the article on learning languages ​​published in this column on February 7th and 8th.)

Tianjin Defeats Hong Kong

Unexpected Defeat Amidst Great Momentum: Hong Kong has suffered two defeats, not confined to being surrounded by enemies, but losing in the midst of great momentum. Yesterday's match between Tianjin and Hong Kong was particularly evident. When the two armies were fighting, Hong Kong's forwards entered the zone, each showing their skills, and frequently shooting. However, Tianjin's defense was strict, and it was difficult to achieve their goals. They visited again and again, and again and again. Although they were diligent, they did not hit the vital points, and in the end, it did not help the overall situation. Tianjin's army, under the effort of resisting, occasionally looked back, and the forwards were able to enter empty, and go down in one fell swoop, relying entirely on proper use, not on the number of attacks.

Tianjin's Midfield Maintains Victory: Tianjin's goalkeeper's performance yesterday was very satisfactory, saving countless dangerous balls. Midfielder Heil had both a copper head and iron legs. He relied on his head to save the situation twice, which amazed the audience. The left and right assistants did not seem to be effective, so they were greatly oppressed by the enemy, and they stayed for a long time. Fortunately, the inner guards were stronger than before, and loopholes were difficult to find. In the eventful times, they were unharmed. It was due to their strength. The five forwards were sharp, and Jones's achievements were above Johansson. The wings were monitored by people, but they were still able to move as before.

Hong Kong's Goalkeeper Ruins the Overall Situation: Hong Kong's five forwards were all very active, and the left-winger Ho Gart was even more outstanding, with long passes and short passes, all of which were excellent. His shots were accurate and fast, making him the crown of the five forwards. The most dangerous person in the Hong Kong team, left inside Redliff, covered both inside and outside, echoed the left wing, and jointly attacked. The Tianjin team lost its color every time. Right winger Xiaogao Shannu was also as free as before. Dagao Shannu and Tam Kong Pak were still agile, but lacked the final blow, resulting in failure, and they could only sigh helplessly. The three-man center-back line was able to cope with it easily. The left and right inner guards were positioned too far forward. Whenever the Tianjin forwards, who were incomparably fast, broke through, they could not turn around in time. The goalkeeper showed weakness and repeatedly failed. He should bear more than half of the responsibility.

One Goal Each in Ten Minutes: Referee Yue Sau Wing blew the whistle to declare war. Hong Kong kicked off and progressed. After three or four exchanges, Tam Kong Pak dribbled the ball into the zone and passed it diagonally to the center. Tianjin's right inner guard could not take care of it. Dagao Shannu saw the opportunity and made a decisive shot, hitting the goal directly. Hong Kong won this goal in just five minutes. In the blink of an eye, Tianjin's Jones flew in, kicked to the left, and center Roger stepped out in front of the crowd, without thinking, added a kick. Within ten minutes, a 1-1 draw was created. Hong Kong's left-winger, Ho Gart, was still active under strict surveillance. He sent a long ball to the left, and Xiaogao Shannu greeted the ball and attacked the goal. Tianjin's goalkeeper was agile, and bent down to catch it. Tam Kong Pak and Dagao Shannu repeatedly pounced, but they were all saved.

The Forwards Gain the Upper Hand, the Defense is Empty: Hong Kong's right-winger Xiaogao Shannu jumped into the periphery, and the entire line followed in, forming a line formation, surrounding the Tianjin goal. The Tianjin team densely deployed heavy troops, and guarded the key points. At this time, the Hong Kong team's arrogance was incomparable, and the center-back line was also transferred to the front, increasing the attacking power, and the inner guards moved to the center line, remotely responding. Unexpectedly, under the great momentum, a sudden disaster descended. Tianjin's right-winger, Fincher Switzerland, passed and received the ball appropriately. Center Roger carried it and advanced quickly, passing sideways to Jones. There was no one on the left or right. Jones calmly shot in, taking the lead with two to one. Hong Kong worked hard and achieved nothing, which was not as good as Tianjin's three passes and four passes, which immediately succeeded. It was also the difference between good luck and bad luck.

An Occasional Visit Again Announces Victory: Hong Kong's Xiaogao Shannu made a horizontal pass in front of the goal, and Redliff greeted it with his head. Tianjin's goalkeeper pushed it backward, and Xiaogao Shannu took a corner kick, which was excellent, and was headed out by center-back Heil while falling to the ground, resolving the dangerous situation. Taking this opportunity, Tianjin launched a counter-attack. Left-winger Archier passed to the right-winger. The right-winger hit the goal post, bounced to Jones's chest, and shot towards the goal, succeeding again. Tianjin then took the lead with three to one. Xiaogao Shannu was brave and directly attacked the Tianjin goal. The goalkeeper lightly lifted the ball upwards, and the waves calmed down. Hong Kong continued to attack, but was always turned away. In the last attack, Tam Kong Pak had avoided Heil, but the shot hit the goalkeeper's chest. In the first half, Tianjin led 3-1.

Photo of Tianjin and Hong Kong Teams (Taken by Xu Tianzhang)

One Goal Gained Through Hardship: Not long after the start of the second half, Ho Gart entered unnoticed and calmly picked the ball. Around the Tianjin goal, heavy troops defended. The three generals in the middle of the Hong Kong team seemed to be wandering on a forked road, not knowing where to go. The attacking routes were all cut off. Redliff suddenly stood out, but the ball was caught by the goalkeeper again. The attack was fierce and terrifying, and the defense was tight and amazing. Hong Kong's Ho Gart was almost the leader of every attack. At 25 minutes, he picked the ball in front of the goal, and Xiaogao Shannu jumped out of the crowd, leaning forward and heading the ball, falling into the net. The score became two to three.

Fierce Attacks Backfire: Hong Kong, with only one goal behind, became more and more diligent, hoping to seek victory from failure. The courage of the attacks was even more fierce than before, but their unfortunate incidents continued to occur. Dagao Shannu was hit on the head twice, but was still able to fight. Tam Kong Pak was injured in the leg and eventually had to be carried off the field. After Hong Kong was two to three, the armored cavalry came across the field again. Xiaogao Shannu picked the ball, but Tam Kong Pak delayed, and the Tianjin team was able to calmly defend and pass safely. Jones then rode in quickly, and the ball advanced from right to left. Center Roger jumped up and headed the ball, flying into the sky. As time was about to end, Hong Kong attacked very quickly, and the left side performed particularly well. The picked balls were endless. There were two sharp shots, launched 15 yards in front of the Tianjin goal, all of which were blocked by Heil with his bald head. The situation suddenly changed. Tianjin's Johansson broke into the territory alone, and the Hong Kong goalkeeper personally resisted. Roger continued to advance and scored another goal. As a result, Tianjin won Hong Kong 4-2.

Overall Trend of Championships Over the Years

This is the Second Grand Event: The term "interport competition" was created in 1908. The Shanghai and Hong Kong Western Football Clubs were the main participants. The first Hong Kong-Shanghai competition was held in Hong Kong, and five years later, in 1913, it was moved to Shanghai. It was suspended for several years due to the European War. In 1924, Hankou sent a team to Shanghai to participate once. Since then, it seems to have become a swan song. It is unknown when it will be able to restore its former glory. In 1928, Tianjin began to compete with Shanghai in interport games. In 1930, Hong Kong, Tianjin, and Shanghai met for the first time in Shanghai, creating an unprecedented grand occasion in the history of interport games. In the following two years, Tianjin remained inactive. In this session, the three heroic divisions met again in Shanghai, which is the second great event of interport games.

The Shanghai Team Still Needs to Work Hard: Looking at the competitions over the years, a statistic shows that Shanghai has played against Hong Kong 14 times, Shanghai has won 9 times, and Hong Kong has won 5 times. Hong Kong has played against Tianjin twice, each winning once. Tianjin has played against Shanghai 4 times, Tianjin has won twice, Shanghai has won once, and drawn once. In addition, Shanghai and Hong Kong have each won against Hankou once. On average, Shanghai has won more than it has lost. In reality, Tianjin's football skills are advancing rapidly, and Hong Kong's talents are emerging one after another. Shanghai cannot be optimistic and still needs to work hard to maintain its glory in the future. The results of previous years are attached on the left:
