Women's Garden

Inaugural Address

— Editor

The wheel of time advances, awakening a group of people who have become numb from hardship. Women are one part of this group. Women all over the world, under immense pressure, are desperately crying out. This has become a historical fact since the late 19th century, and some have already obtained a bright future.

In our country, since the May Fourth Movement, the women's movement has also become an epoch-making page in history. At that time, the number of publications on women's issues was as numerous as bamboo shoots after rain, but they were only fleeting, and soon gradually declined. Is it that Chinese women have already obtained a bright future and do not need to cry out anymore? Unawakened women will certainly stare blankly and not know how to answer, but awakened women will respond sadly and say: (No).

Now, a small number of women have been liberated from the family to the school, and from the school to society. However, the facts they have shown are: most of them have been swept into the path of modernity by the raging waves of the times, participating in what (fashion shows), arranging beautiful new families, only knowing to catch up with Western civilization, thus becoming good customers of imperialist commodities: not only becoming slaves to sell foreign goods, but also becoming modern playthings. Another part of intellectual women are obsessed with the supremacy of love and the supremacy of art, dreaming (love) and (beauty) dreams. As for rural women, they still live a life of hardship like cattle and horses. The female workers in factories in the cities are spending a life of ignorant and laborious life. We have now opened up this small garden, hoping that our compatriots will work together to irrigate it, work hard to cultivate it, and write about what you want to advocate, and tell about all your suffering. We also accept all the well-intentioned instructions of our male compatriots. We hope to live together and operate together on this rugged path of life.

Hurry Up and Open Up the Women's Garden!

— Bi Yao

Where is the women's garden? Looking all over the country, most women are subordinate. Women used to have no place to stand, because of this, they bound their small feet like awls; now, although it is said that they have been liberated, they only have a pair of empty seven-inch unbound feet.

Women are already extremely docile sheep, and women are already the most dilapidated and foolish creatures. For the sake of food, clothing, and housing, they sell their flesh piecemeal (prostitutes) or wholesale (marry); for the sake of having no chance to learn, or having some knowledge but not daring to act directly because they are not their own masters, they sell their souls; finally, they use hands without souls to deal with the current world or nurture future lives, and sell their race.

In the old society, although women did not have an independent garden, they were still attached to men, cooking and managing the home, raising silkworms and picking tea, helping with hard work. But in the new society, modern women have revolutionized these works: the canon they worship is wearing, eating, and carefree. Thus, they have become bees and butterflies in the men's garden, and to put it more badly, they have become foxes. In a dilapidated society like China, how much energy can men have to cultivate? Moreover, adding to the disturbance of these bees and butterflies, and the gnawing of the foxes?

It is not that women absolutely have no garden, just as it is not that China has no vast land; however, half has already been exploited by others, and half is being abandoned by themselves.

What is most heartbreaking is the self-abandonment of women in the new era. For the sake of enjoyment, comfort, and parasitism, they are willing to watch the country sink deeper and deeper, and men are increasingly oppressed by two kinds of people, while they retreat to the inhuman status of bees, butterflies, and foxes.

We never talk about the big problems of the world and humanity. In the current country, the women's garden that needs to be opened up urgently has at least these works: saving the flesh of commodities, making them independent and self-respecting; saving the dim souls, making them smart and clean; saving the dying race, making them great and long-lasting.

Our garden, which has been exploited by others, undoubtedly needs to be taken back quickly; as for those that have been abandoned by ourselves, it is too lacking in (human) flavor not to work hard to take them back. We must always shout loudly: (Hurry up and open up the women's garden)!

Whose (Women's Garden)?

— Minzhi

Because China has produced too many Ah Qs, the position of women in society is simply regarded as something unnecessary. Originally, the scholars and officials of ancient China regarded women as dangerous goods: and the Chinese Ah Qs all took it upon themselves to be (saints) and (omnipotent doctors), so the position of women in society was especially completely denied. On the stage of all Chinese historical dramas, palace maids, queens, and Lin Daiyu disguised as old actors can be (performed,) which shows that in the eyes of the country where Ah Qs are rampant, women have been regarded as something that can be disguised, because Ah Qs are all omnipotent doctors, and Ah Qs all have the skills of women.

Therefore, when talking about opening up (women's garden,) today, how can one not be filled with emotion?

The wife layer, Miss layer, and what (flower) and (queen) layer of Chinese women are all in the business of X.

(Women's garden) is naturally (men are not allowed in,) and among women, it seems that not everyone can come in. It is hoped that this place will exclude the mood of the wife-like (bored and unhappy going to the park to relax) and entertain, for women who produce for society and can fight for real life to participate in this amateur park.

It is hoped that this place will strictly abandon articles discussing how to please men in order to win men's favors. On the contrary, it should provide historical materials of working women in actual life, and discuss how to obtain social equality and re-evaluate the contribution of women to society.

Ellen Key and Alexandra Kollontai

— Zi

Ellen Key and Alexandra Kollontai are pioneers in the women's world, and both have unique insights into the issue of women's liberation. Below is a record of the conversation about them.

Zi Wen: Today, the topic we are preparing to discuss is: (Ellen Key and Alexandra Kollontai).

Ying Ying: Isn't Alexandra Kollontai the Soviet female writer who wrote (Three Generations of Love) and (Red Bird, etc.)?

Zi Wen: She is not only a writer, but also a diplomat. She has served as the ambassador to Norway and the ambassador to Mexico.

Fei Pei: The words and deeds of these two women in the world are indeed worthy of our study. It's just that I don't understand the life and deeds of these two people. Now I will raise what I don't understand and ask you to teach me: In which country was Ellen Key born?

Zi Wen: She was born in 1849 in a small city in southern Sweden. Her father once served as a cabinet member. Her mother was also highly educated and very enthusiastic about women's liberation, so Ellen Key's later promotion of the women's liberation movement was not without reason.

Fei Pei: What is Ellen Key's outlook on life?

Zi Wen: She is a spiritual optimist. She believes that since she is born in this world, her mind and body should be very healthy, very happy, and live powerfully. She said: (Our life should be full of humility, a broad mind, a deep understanding of all things like a great poet, and always be as innocent, happy and lively as a child.) From these words, we can imagine how bright, humble, broad and generous her outlook on life is.

Ying Ying: Looking at it this way, Ellen Key is just a person who compromises with reality.

Zi Wen: That can't be said either. If she was a realistic compromiser, how could she have shouted the call for (liberating women) in that era? However, she uses (love) to reconcile life, neither blaming the sky nor hating people, and at the same time is definitely not a realistic compromiser but a rebel. She is also not like ordinary women who are dissatisfied with real life, but still sink into real life and cannot extricate themselves.

Fei Pei: What are the goals of Ellen Key's women's movement?

Zi Wen: She put forward three creeds. 1. Marriage should be based on love. 2. Free divorce. 3. Maternal revival.

Ying Ying: I remember that Ellen Key's advocacy of love marriage is based on eugenics. Is that right?

Zi Wen: Yes. She once said: (Love is sacred and is the source of all culture. The two sides of love marriage must feel supreme happiness, and the children born under such a life must be smarter than the children born to ordinary couples without love. However, Ellen Key's view is indeed lacking scientific basis. She only said that most of the so-called great men, great artists, and great thinkers in history are illegitimate children, in other words, their parents are mostly combined by love. (To be continued)

The Struggle for Women's Suffrage in the World

— Jing

Since the late 19th century, women in various countries around the world have wanted to have equal status with men in politics. Therefore, women in various countries mostly regard obtaining suffrage as the prerequisite for the liberation movement. The countries that have successively obtained suffrage are listed below:

Australia 1893 Finland 1906

Norway 1915 Denmark 1915

Netherlands 1917 Soviet Union 1917

United Kingdom 1918 Germany 1919

Hungary 1919

South America 1919 United States 1920

Poland 1921 Sweden 1921

Canada 1921 Greece 1930

Spain 1931

As for women in France, Japan, Italy, Switzerland, Romania, and other countries, although they already have a considerable status in society, and they are also constantly campaigning for the acquisition of political power, they have not been allowed by the rulers.

The Life of a Woman

— Xuanwen

In this arena of increasingly fierce survival competition, it is not easy to covet life. But people are always greedy for life and afraid of death. To live, one must live healthily. Weak and sickly bodies cannot play a good role on this stage of life. To have a healthy body, it is固 due to constant training and health maintenance, but the congenital is also important. In today's world where human beings have not yet obtained other methods to preserve the race, the health of the mother is even more important. A healthy mother has a healthy fetus; a healthy fetus can easily grow up. After growing up, it can become a healthy citizen. Therefore, the health of a woman's life is not only necessary for her personal survival, but also closely related to the future of national survival. The points that should be paid attention to in (The Life of a Woman) are presented to the readers in paragraphs.

1. Sexual Buds

Byron knew about love at the age of eight, and Dante had a lover at the age of nine. Most smart people are precocious. Under such circumstances, what mothers should pay special attention to is: When does the child's sexual bud occur, and how is it expressed? It all depends on the mother's careful understanding in silent observation and guidance.

When a child's sexual bud first occurs, the most important thing for mothers to pay attention to is whether the child has (self-smear) behavior. Even when children are three or four years old and are still learning to walk, such behavior can cause them to develop indelible bad habits due to certain sensations.

Special attention should be paid to: Whether the child is suffering from pinworms丨丨a small worm that often parasitizes at the anus, which can cause the child's anus to itch strangely丨丨because pinworms often like to come out of the anus at night to lay eggs. When it goes back, if it accidentally enters the child's genitals, it will definitely feel itchy and scratch. Scratching will definitely feel pleasure, thus forming the habit of (self-smear). In addition, there are also cases where the child does not clean it after urination, which will eventually lead to strange itching. Scratching can also become the bad habit of (self-smear). However, children in this period are all innocent and lively, and it is a great time to educate them. If the mother can discover her bad habits and give appropriate hints and guidance early, it is not difficult to correct them. In case the mother does not pay attention to her or lets her go, making her develop a habit that she cannot control, and when she reaches the age of breaking her melon, when the spring green blood runs in the fallopian tubes, and at the same time, due to the action of internal secretions, instinctual sexual impulses arise, at this time, the aforementioned bad habits have been difficult to correct, affecting the person's lifelong happiness and health, and even suffering from infertility. Those who are mothers in the world cannot but pay attention to this.

Amateur Weekly

Casual Chats in Leisure Time

Genius Labyrinth

— Shao Wen

In the course of history, many great inventors have appeared. People understand these inventors as (geniuses), believing that their intelligence, wisdom, and talent are innate, saying that they are fundamentally different from ordinary people. If anyone wants to disagree with this, then people with this view will immediately ask: Why could only Watt invent the steam engine, only Stephenson invent the train, only Fulton invent the steamboat, and not others? Isn't this proof that inventors are different from ordinary people?

True, all great inventors are geniuses, and most of them are more intelligent than the average person, but this is only one factor that makes it possible for them to become inventors. What makes this possibility a reality is the environment in which they are situated. Although Watt was intelligent, he would not have been able to invent the steam engine if he had not been an apprentice mechanic and a machinist for the steam engine at the University of Glasgow. Stephenson and Fulton's becoming inventors of trains and steamboats is also inextricably linked to the environment in which they lived.

At the same time, the level of development of social culture is the main condition that determines what kind of inventors all great inventors become. No matter how intelligent a person is, even if his personal living environment is very good, his achievements cannot exceed the level of cultural development of the society in which he lives. Although Kongming was intelligent, he could only invent wooden oxen and flowing horses in the Three Kingdoms period, and could not build trains and steamships; even with the skill of Gongshuzi, he could not build modern-style Western-style houses in the Warring States period; even Watt, Stephenson, and Fulton, as extraordinary as they were, could not have invented huge electric machines in the eighteenth century.

Furthermore, the demands of the era and society are also constraints on the achievements of all inventors. Watt's invention of the steam engine, Stephenson's invention of the train, and Fulton's invention of the steamboat all emerged with the collapse of feudal society and the growth of modern (civilized society) since the Renaissance. Because modern (cultural society) is built on the foundation of industry and commerce, it needs steam engines, trains, steamboats, etc., so Watt, Stephenson, Fulton, etc. invented them. Watt and others were merely inventors who responded to this need, not superhuman beings above all else. Moreover, we can also say that even without Watt and the like, at most the development of modern (civilized society) would be delayed for some time, but there is no question that this society would inevitably emerge and develop.

Therefore, the talents and achievements of all great inventors are given to them by society and the era, not something innate. They are the same as ordinary people, they are people of the era, people of society, not some (monsters) beyond the era and beyond society. The reason why they can specially invent something among a number of people is mainly because they have a suitable living environment, can see the needs of society and the era, and can work hard under these needs. There is really nothing mysterious or incomprehensible about it.

This theory can not only explain all great inventors, but also be used to explain all great political, academic, and artistic geniuses. The labyrinth of genius can thus be completely opened.

Of course, this is only a scientific understanding of all great inventors and geniuses, and does not deny their contributions to human society.

Life

Opening Festival Money

— Fei Qiusheng

I, I am a naive virgin who has not experienced the world. Now I am a minor employee in the XX factory who seems important but is not important, 丨丨 a very, very minor employee. In the minds of my colleagues, there is indeed no such human-like impression. As for me, I also feel that I am not self-respecting enough, and I am always accepting all commands with all my heart, as if this is indeed iron-cast in my fate.

The XX factory is very large, and the workers account for about 96% of the total number of employees. Because the work is very noble, their lives are also above all the workers. Therefore, their horizons and their family fortunes are also tied to their foreheads.

Shusheng is the teaboy in the manager's office 丨丨 a relative of the manager, 丨丨 is a snobbish villain. His salary is more than twice mine, no wonder he shouts and bullies others, relying on his power.

Speaking of my position, it is ultimately one step higher than Shusheng, but it is very difficult to get him to do things. Not only does he not respond to you, but he also gives you an extra fierce look to embarrass you, and sometimes he gives you a sour feeling.

(Hey 丨 Shusheng 丨 Please send this to Mr. Wang, okay?) I said to Shusheng with a smile.

(Who has time? No time 丨 You can go yourself 丨) He put on a straight face and grumbled with a chain of answers.

(Hey 丨 Shusheng! Please ask Mr. Wang to come 丨) Then came the manager's instructions.

(Oh 丨 Oh 丨 Oh 丨 Okay 丨········· Shusheng responded repeatedly and left.

(Shusheng 丨 Then take it to him 丨)

(No 丨 No 丨 I still have to go somewhere else 丨) This is obviously an unreasonable excuse.

But I can't vent my anger as much as possible, I can only open my mouth wide and swallow this sour and spicy feeling. To whom should I complain?

The lunar New Year's Day is approaching again. According to our factory rules, a double salary will be given when paying wages once at the end of the year. Of course, this time will be no exception 丨

I remember it was a bright morning, and the sound of the machines in the factory was already rumbling. I stepped into the director's office and ran into Shusheng head-on.

(Oh 丨 Good morning 丨 Mr. X 丨) This is Shusheng's rare compliment to me. I also inexplicably replied a few times: (Good morning 丨 Good morning 丨 Good morning 丨) He took the teapot to make tea.

The coal in the stove was burning red, moving the entire room out of the cold. At that time, I was the first to arrive in the director's office, and everything was silent, only the raging coal was playing a disjointed tune. Today's special image in the room surprised me at a glance: the things on the desk were always disorganized, but today they were all neatly organized; the dust on the desk was always brushed off with a feather duster, and sometimes it was not brushed at all, but today they were all wiped brightly. Is this a good sign?

Shusheng's tea has been brewed.

(Mr. X 丨 Have some tea 丨) Shusheng put a cup of steaming tea on my desk.

Shusheng's actions and expression today really made me feel surprised. Has he changed? Has he repented?

Everyone knows today is the day to pay double wages, and it's also Saturday, so everyone's faces are full of smiles. The staff in the director's office didn't do anything all day, just talked. The telephone next to the wall was very busy. This one went to find Miss so-and-so, that one went to make an appointment with Ms. so-and-so, and some even suggested opening a room, anyway, tomorrow is Sunday, so they can have a good time. The workers also didn't feel like working. Some people smiled, but most people didn't, they had a group of creditors following them, so they didn't seem happy.

The morning passed in such a blur, and the 5 o'clock that everyone was looking forward to arrived, and the working machines also stopped turning. The workers washed their faces, put on their clothes, and prepared to leave, but the wages had not yet been distributed. The dismissal bell had already rung, and the director's office was immediately crowded with Narma Wens from various departments, inquiring about wages.

Outside the door stood many, many people, almost blocking the alley. What are they doing? They are the workers' creditors.

The clock on the wall had struck six, but the person who distributes the wages had not yet arrived. The workers were standing on the escalators on each floor, all looking at the door of the director's office in unison.

At this time, the manager also became anxious and made six or seven calls to the bank in a row, but nothing happened.

Finally, at half past six, the person from the bank who was sent to distribute the wages arrived. In an instant, the director's office was packed

Page 22

water couldn't leak through, and people pushed and shoved to be the first. The legs of the desks were each moved more than half a foot.

It wasn't until 7 o'clock that the wages were finally distributed, and the people from the bank also left. At that time, all the staff in the director's office had not yet run away.

(Shusheng 丨 Please use these to buy some wine to drink!) The manager handed a ten-yuan bill to Shusheng and said.

(Oh! Oh! Oh! Thank you 丨 Mr. X 丨) Shusheng thanked him.

At this time, my brain suddenly became clever; it turned out that Shusheng was so kind today because of·········

One by one, Shusheng received the festival money, and then it was my turn. My heart kept jumping non-stop: my brain was constantly thinking about······

(Ah 丨 If I have to give him four yuan, then I would never want to in my life, and I don't have this money. The double wages I received are not enough for the family's New Year's meals. If I give him two yuan 丨 then if people see it, it will be too stingy. People are giving him four yuan, six yuan, eight yuan. But, no 丨 no 丨 My salary is smaller than others, maybe it won't happen 丨)

But when I looked up and saw his kind and amiable expression today, my heart softened again. Other people's eyes were all focused on me, and my hands couldn't help but tremble.

At this time, most of the people in the director's office had left, so my courage grew again; his usual fierce face also vaguely appeared in my eyes; the sour feelings I had suffered also generally churned out of my chest.

(No 丨 I must give him two yuan 丨) I decided in my heart.

(Shusheng 丨 These are nothing, go have a smoke 丨) I stiffened my head and handed him a two-yuan bill.

(Oh 丨·········· Thank you!) Shusheng took the money, paused, and his eyes darted around a few times.

My face flushed red, and I lowered my head and slipped out in a puff of smoke.

Famous People's Speeches

Mr. Zhang Yousan's Speech (The Temporality of Youth Cultivation)

— Notes by Shen Pinru

The explanation of the two words "cultivation" is that on the one hand, people are dissatisfied with reality, and on the other hand, they want to improve their various aspects, constantly striving towards the direction of improving ideals. This direction is what is called cultivation.

(1) Maxims and cultivation use a concise and generalized language as a standard. Usually, maxims are based on the experiences of all successful people who are higher than us as our role models, and are always flawless, but there are also mistakes. For example, (being wise and protecting oneself) is based on personal interests as a prerequisite without regard to the welfare of the public. This is to tell you not to be silly, to sacrifice oneself for the sake of the public, causing many energetic and enterprising youths to become timid and decadent. For example, (serving as an official when the country is prosperous, and retreating when the country is in turmoil) is simply speculation. However, there are many good maxims, but they cannot be used as a model for the entire life. For example, in terms of the country (everyone is responsible for the rise and fall of the world), this is only a slogan for civic life and cannot take care of the specifics. Therefore, although maxims can help us cultivate ourselves, because the basis is inappropriate or only focuses on one aspect, they cannot serve as a model for the entire life.

(2) Moral principles and cultivation The ancients put forward many words as the goals of cultivation, such as benevolence, righteousness, loyalty, filial piety, diligence, frugality, respect, love, etc. These many moral principles were set by different people and are fundamentally different. How can we learn from them? Moreover, these are abstract and can be hung on the wall to warn us, but they cannot be used as cultivation for the entire life. In addition, these moral principles are also undefined. In ancient times, someone asked Confucius, (How can one be filial?), he said: (Do not violate one's parents for three years). Later he said: (Serve them with propriety when they are alive, bury them with propriety when they die, and sacrifice to them with propriety). Later he said: (Provide them with food and drink), and finally said: (Be respectful in demeanor to be filial). Such moral principles are all empty and not specific. Dr. Sun Yat-sen advocated loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, faith, righteousness, and peace. He also said that they should be promoted and carried forward in accordance with the trend of the times and based on scientific principles, so moral principles are empty and insufficient.

(3) Hero worship and cultivation In youth, people are full of worship. When they encounter or read about successful great men, heroes, and outstanding people in literature, science, politics, and military affairs in books, they always worship them wholeheartedly and use the fine deeds of heroes and great men as our imitation. Although this is specific and whole, and can avoid the bias of maxims and the emptiness of moral principles, there are also two shortcomings: One is external. Heroes are created by the times. It is the need of the times and the urgency of the environment that create them. The second is internal. His innate knowledge, talent, and temperament are particularly high compared to ordinary people. Can another Liu Bei or Yue Fei appear in the Warring States period or the Song Dynasty, or in the present when the times have changed several times? Moreover, Liu Bei's loyalty to one person, although Yue Fei fought for the nation, but he retreated when he received the emperor's order in an emergency, because obedience was more important than fighting against foreign enemies. This is sticking to the monarch. It can be seen that hero worship is not perfect.

(4) The Temporality of Cultivation Based on the above three points, a definition can be obtained, that is, cultivation has temporality. For example, in the Eastern Jin Dynasty, emphasis was placed on Qingtan. All scholars and officials were eloquent and eloquent, but now they are regarded as empty talk and doing nothing. The Song Dynasty was about studying the principles of human nature. If you talked thoroughly, you could become a high official, but it doesn't work now. There is also a saying (The highest virtue is not to speak wildly or act recklessly). This is in terms of China, and there are also some in foreign countries. For example, they must use Latin when writing articles or talking, and they also worship the strange behaviors of samurai and monks. They lock their bodies in the open air, do not eat or drink for several days, and let the sun shine and rain drench them. He said: (A person who can endure the hardship of the flesh will definitely improve his personality.) These are all times that fascinate them, and this kind of cultivation is the most appropriate in this era.

Diligent Life

— Jing Ye

(Diligence) is amazing. Many geniuses have used (diligence) to create their works. The Spanish poet Lope de Vega diligently wrote about 2,000 kinds of plays, of which only 500 kinds can be passed down to our time. In addition, he also has other works in 21 volumes and many other poems. The French bookseller Levy was the publisher of many works by the great writer Alexandre Dumas. According to the bookseller's catalogue alone, there are already as many as 300 volumes of these works, but this catalogue is still incomplete. Another example is the female writer George Sand. There is a legend about her that after finishing a novel at two o'clock in the night, she put a pack of blank paper in front of her seat in order to write the first few chapters of another new work. Her surviving works total 109 volumes. The famous mathematician Leonhard Euler has at least 30,000 pages of printed matter in his original manuscripts. In these printed matters, every line is filled with the most difficult problems that people can think of. He was also a particularly good memory. It is said that he memorized the entire book (Odyssey and Iliad) in twenty-two days. In addition, there is the great writer Goethe, whose complete works have now been published in a total of 130 volumes.

Speeches

Women and Clothing

— Ci Yuan

Recently, the criticism about women, especially female students (presumably because they are the backbone of the intellectual citizens), that has been talked about the most is the issue of clothing. Because of this, some have issued very stern criticisms, saying that it is Europeanization and luxury. Some angrily say that schools should be closed, saying that this is indeed a phenomenon that cannot be ignored in society. In the current situation where my country's industries are declining and people are living in poverty, the luxury and Europeanization of female students' clothing is accelerating the demise of Chinese society.

Originally, things that were not very serious have become serious after their accusations and criticisms. Now let us study this so-called (serious) matter without prejudice, shall we?

The occurrence and existence of every phenomenon in society has its own basis and background for its occurrence and existence. There is a relationship between cause and effect. There will never be anything that comes out of thin air without a cause. According to this, let us grasp why women's clothing is becoming more and more luxurious. Finally, let's take a look at whether the luxury of women's clothing is, as some people say, the biggest reason for preventing social progress and endangering the country and nation.

We know that under the current social system, the main phenomenon is that everything is becoming commercialized and capitalized. In the process of the transition from feudal system to the current system, women have always been regarded as a part of men's private property. Therefore, when everything becomes commercialized, women are also seen as special commodities. Under the violent oppression of cunning men, women have no room for resistance. The fragile women can only endure humiliation and obey. The oppression of the social environment and the intentional coercion of men have forced them to embark on the path of luxury to increase the price of commodities. What a tragic fact! The luxury of clothing is the oppression of the social environment and the fault of men. It is futile to only make sarcastic jokes, criticisms, and accusations without improving the existing social system and examining one's own faults.

To retreat and talk about the current luxury of women's clothing, especially female students, it is not necessarily a very serious sin, and it is not necessarily the great treason that some people say that prevents public progress and endangers the country. We know that human beings are rational animals and have an innate instinct to love beauty. The development of this instinct is higher in women than in men. As human knowledge progresses, the concept of aesthetics develops even more. As far as men are concerned, I believe that among those who criticize and blame, there must be many who wear high-end suits and silk jackets, so why shouldn't women wear red and green? Is it because not being luxurious and not wearing red and green means expressing patriotism and advocating domestic products? Just look at the facts in society, I am afraid that those who are outwardly simple are big traitors and sellers of foreign goods! As long as they are truly studying knowledge, what is the use of cold ridicule?

Scientific Talks

Scientific Statistics

— Chu Mo Translator

(1) Gold and silver in seawater

Seawater contains large amounts of dissolved gold and silver. In one million grams of seawater, we can extract six thousandths of a gram of gold and nineteen thousandths of a gram of silver. It is estimated that the value of gold in seawater is as high as 58.38 trillion marks, and the value of silver is 5.3 trillion marks. Therefore, if we divide these gold and silver equally among the 1.6 billion people on Earth, each person can get 3.5 million marks of gold and 320,000 marks of silver.

(2) Vocabulary of various texts

The various different words or terms needed by people who have received secondary education usually do not exceed two to three thousand. The book (Old Testament) contains about 5,800 different words, the (New Testament) 4,100, Homer's (Odyssey and Iliad) 9,000, Milton's complete works 8,000, and French contains up to 110,000 words, while English has 120,000 words. In addition, Grimm's (Complete German Dictionary), after he supplemented it, can contain about 500,000 different words, terms, or phrases, and all proper names are not included.

(3) Lifespan of animals and plants

Some animals usually live much longer than humans. For example, some shellfish have a lifespan of 100 years, parrots, eagles, vultures, swans, and bald eagles are all over 100 years old, and carp, elephants, and whales are 200 years old. But the longest-lived animal is probably the tortoise. There is a living tortoise in the artillery barracks in Mauritius. It is estimated that it is already 300 years old. A tortoise died in the London Zoo in 1906. It weighed 500 pounds and it was estimated it was 400 years old. During its lifetime, it ate more feed in the summer than a cow needed, but it fasted in the winter. In 1911, someone caught a tortoise and found words left on its back, but these words were left in 1793.

Some trees also live for a very long time. There was such a tree in India (but it has now fallen), and according to the scientists' judgment, it sprouted more than 7,000 years ago. In that case, when Abraham Lincoln was alive, it had already lived for several millennia

International Broadcasting Radio Station

World Rare News

— Qi Cheng

In Berlin, there is an electrical robot that stands on the street and can guide passers-by with directions and answer 180 questions without error.

A village in England named (Tang) Tong still maintains the civilization of the 17th century. There are no cinemas, no gas stations, and even no car roads to the outside world. The female postmaster there is also the only school principal there, and the school has two students. It turns out that there are only 100 residents in this village.

According to recent research results in the scientific community, bees cannot see red, but bees can see ultraviolet rays that are beyond human eyesight.

German inventor A. Rohrback is now designing a new type of aircraft that can move forward or backward, or stay motionless in the air, as the driver wishes.

There is a poisonous lake in Panama called (Dead Lake). The bones of birds and animals are piled around the lake, all of which died after tasting the water in the lake. People who drink it cannot escape death either. Therefore, the locals do not want to get close to this lake. The reason why this lake is poisonous is because the stones at the bottom of the lake contain arsenic.

According to a report by three scientists from an American dairy company, the amount of vitamin A contained in milk and butter depends entirely on whether the hay eaten by the cow is good.

An American named John of Forton has recently built a coal-powered car. It is said that this car can travel 93 kilometers per hour (approximately 167 li in Chinese miles).

Three sources of oil that can supply 20,000 tons of oil per day have recently been discovered in the Caucasus.

According to the results of experiments by Dr. D.A. Laird of Colgateo University in the United States: Short but comfortable sleep is actually more effective than long but restless sleep.

In 1932, the Soviet Union published more than 300 million books on science. It is said that it has exceeded the number of books published in Germany, France, England, Italy, and the United States.

Someone recently invented a new method for baking sweet potatoes: before baking, first put the sweet potatoes in hot water for fifteen minutes, and then take them out to bake, which can reduce the baking time by half.

The largest locomotive factory in Europe has recently been completed in Ukraine. The factory can manufacture 1,800 locomotives per year. This type of locomotive can tow 2,000 tons of freight cars at a very high speed.

Special Self-Employment Introduction

Army Captain

— Scholar

丨丨Until now, useless in everything

Just begging for food in the world 丨丨

I am a scholar. I started working at the age of twenty, and now I am forty-two. In these twenty-two years, although I have experienced unemployment, this is the first time I have been unemployed for such a long period.

Speaking of this unemployment, it is somewhat unjust. I was originally a captain secretary in a certain regiment. Because that regiment was going to Jiangxi, my family, seeing that I was no longer young, did not want me to travel far to Jiangxi, and told me to resign. Who knew that this resignation would plunge me into famine. From August last year until now, I have not been able to find a job. At that time, it was said that Jiangxi was too far away and dangerous; but now, there is no way to go anywhere, and there is no place further away. All that remains is the danger of hunger, approaching day by day. The old wife needs to be supported, and the young children need to be fed, but the falling snowflakes cannot be used as clothing, and the falling tears cannot be exchanged for rice. Seeking friends, friends avoid you; seeking relatives, it is still the same as running into a wall.

Because I am a scholar, I have no other skills, only having learned a good hand of Zhao calligraphy that everyone loves. Running script is used for writing letters, and regular script is used for copying official documents, but what is the use? Submitting articles is not easy, and it is even more difficult to exchange for money to buy rice immediately. If you can write a good official document, no one asks you now, and it is worthless. The Book of Poetry and Confucius' sayings certainly cannot be exchanged for money, and social democracy cannot bring rice. This is the skill of a scholar, and now I want to exchange it for a meal in the world. I wonder who needs this skill?

Incidentally, because I have a family, living expenses should be at least forty yuan, and board and lodging are required. I am healthy and have no habits, which should also be stated here. Please forward correspondence through this publication.
